Decision to Establish the Headquarters of the Deputy Commanders of the Army, Navy, and Air Force in Beiping

▲ Zhu Guangmu Internally Designated as Secretary-General

Liu Guang Carries Tables of Organization and Seals to Zhang Xueliang

From a correspondent in Fan Yang: The issue of establishing the headquarters of the deputy commanders of the Army, Navy, and Air Force has been under discussion for a long time without clear resolution. Since Zhang Xueliang returned to Shenyang, the matter has been decided through discussions with various key figures and correspondence with the central government. General Commander Chiang sent Liu Guang, Director of the National Defense Department of the General Staff, to deliver the tables of organization and seals for the headquarters of the deputy commanders. Liu arrived in Shenyang on the 1st of this month. According to reports, the headquarters of the deputy commanders will be established in Beiping. Zhang will go to Beiping to organize its establishment after the lunar new year. The headquarters will be organized into seven departments: staff, secretariat, general affairs, military law, military medical, adjutant, and logistics. There will also be two chiefs of staff and secretariat. The seven departments will have a total of over 200 personnel, who will be announced by Deputy Commander Zhang soon. It is rumored that Zhu Guangmu has been internally designated as the Secretary-General. The monthly budget will be 50,000 or 60,000 yuan, which has not yet been decided. The authority of the headquarters is to act on behalf of the commander-in-chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force and to implement military matters in the provinces of Hebei, Shanxi, Chahar, Suiyuan, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. The headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force in Nanjing will be abolished, and a general commander's office will be established in Beiping. Deputy Commander Zhang will also establish a deputy commander's office in Shenyang. The organization of the office will be simple, with personnel concurrently serving from the Border Defense Command. The Border Defense Command will naturally remain in existence, but it is rumored to be undergoing reorganization and is currently under planning. It is reported that after assuming the position of deputy commander, Zhang Xueliang will spend one-third of his time in Beiping handling the affairs of the headquarters of the deputy commanders and two-thirds of his time handling the affairs of the Northeast Border Defense. Zhang will continue to concurrently serve as the commander of the Northeast Border Defense. The rumor that Zhang will focus solely on the position of deputy commander and appoint Zhang Zuoxiang as the commander of the Border Defense is inaccurate. (February 6)

Northern Financial Conference Postponed

Shenyang News, The Northern Financial Conference, originally scheduled to last for ten days, has been extended due to the large number of proposals. In the past ten days, the conference has reached decisions and discussed the results of cases, and nine items have been published. (1) Income and expenditure, the division between the state and local boundaries should be clearly demarcated to avoid confusion. Chairman Zhang Xueliang submitted for discussion. (2) Division of income and expenditure between the state and local levels, Liaoning Finance Director Zhang Zhenlu proposed that the above two cases be discussed together. The meeting decided to follow the standards promulgated by the ministry in the 17th year. (3) Please order the national tax collection agency to abolish the system of commercial contracting. Jing Youyan, special commissioner of finance in Hebei, proposed that all contracted donations and taxes, whether they belong to the country or to the local government, should be abolished and directly collected by the official authorities. Those who are restricted by conditional contracts due to unexpired terms may temporarily maintain the status quo, but should still be abolished upon expiration. (4) Unify the consumption tax rate and no longer re-levy after a single tax. Liaoning Finance Director Zhang Zhenlu proposed. After discussion, the special consumption tax rates should be consistent across the eastern provinces. The specific detailed tax items should be discussed separately. (5) Prepare and present personal opinions on the estate tax and income tax. Jing Youyan, special commissioner of finance in Hebei, proposed. (6) Proposal to prepare estate tax. Liaoning Finance Director Zhang Zhenlu proposed. (7) Proposal to prepare income tax. Liaoning Finance Director Zhang Zhenlu proposed. The above three cases were discussed together. It was decided that, according to the current situation, it is imperative to implement both the income and estate taxes and that all difficulties should be overcome. Request the ministry's approval to have one year to prepare the estate tax and six months to prepare the income tax. (8) Proposal to restrict tax exemptions. Liaoning Finance Director Zhang Zhenlu proposed. It was decided that tax-exempt items should comply with central regulations. Tax-exempt permits should be issued by the financial authorities. (9) The provinces and cities in the Northeast region follow the orders of the Executive Yuan to abolish transit dues and reform the unified tax, special tax, and business tax. There are preliminary issues and subsequent issues. Please decide on the specific articles and publicize the decision. Jilin Finance Director Ronghou proposed. A, preliminary issues. 1. It is necessary to first designate which of the old donations and taxes in the provinces and cities of the Northeast should be recognized as transit dues and which should be recognized as similar to transit dues, so that it is known which should be abolished and which should not be abolished. Only after the types to be abolished have been determined can the estimated amount of loss be known. Should the provinces and cities in the Northeast each submit a detailed list of the donations and taxes to be abolished for review? This should be decided first. After discussion, each province and city will submit a detailed list of the tax items to be abolished for review and submit them within one or two days. 1. Abolishing transit dues and similar transit dues. The old donations and taxes of each province and city have inherent losses, and there are also losses from reforming the unified tax and special tax. There are inherent losses in national taxes and provincial local taxes, and there are also losses in county local taxes. Should the various losses be divided into separate lists for review? This should be decided first. After discussion, separate lists of the total amounts of national taxes, provincial local taxes, and county local taxes should be prepared and submitted within two days. 1. The ministry has designated five types of goods subject to the unified tax and nineteen types of goods subject to special consumption tax. What types of goods subject to the unified tax and what types of goods subject to special consumption tax are currently available in each province and city? It is not possible to have all of them or none of them. Should a list be prepared for review? This should be decided first. After discussion, the original designated types and estimated tax amounts, as well as the proposed additional types and tax amounts, should be submitted to the review committee. Please submit them within one or two days. 1. Among the five types of unified tax designated by the ministry, only the tax rates for cigarettes and wheat flour are fixed. The tax rates for the remaining three types (matches, cement, and cotton yarn) have not been promulgated. Should we wait for the ministry's regulations to be promulgated before complying, or should the committee first review and unify the regulations? This should be decided first. It was decided that we should wait for the ministry's regulations to be promulgated before verifying and implementing them.

Zhang Huizan Killed in Ji'an

▲ Head Transported to the Provincial Capital for Burial

Nanchang Dispatch: Zhang Huizan, commander of the 18th Division of the Ninth Route Army, formerly the main force in the central route for suppressing Zhu and Mao, led the 52nd and 53rd Brigades on New Year's Eve last year, taking the lead and penetrating deep into the enemy's lair when advancing from Donggu to Xingguo. However, due to the dense mountains and winding paths, when they reached Longgang, Zhu and Mao's main bandit forces had already occupied the high ground and surrounded the officers and soldiers. Commander Zhang, facing overwhelming numerical disadvantage and impassable roads, eventually ran out of ammunition and reinforcements. Commander Zhang was then captured by the bandits. According to a clerk who escaped from the 104th Regiment of the 52nd Brigade, after Commander Zhang was taken to the bandit lair in Xingguo, Zhu and Mao initially treated him well and repeatedly tried to persuade him to surrender officers and soldiers and trick them into handing over weapons and ammunition. Zhang remained unyielding. Zhu and Mao, realizing that Zhang was difficult to use, held a false central meeting and decided to kill Commander Zhang on the 28th of last month in Futian (on the border of Ji'an) and cut off his head, placing it in the Jishui River to float downstream. On the 2nd of this month, sentries from the 77th Division saw a large one-sided plaque from the Zhang clan ancestral hall floating downstream on the Ji'an River, covered with red cloth. They retrieved it and saw a human head placed on top, labeled as Commander Zhang's head, along with reactionary propaganda and rebellious slogans. The sentries then took the head to Ji'an City, where it was identified by former members of the 18th Division and Zhang's relatives as Zhang's head without a doubt. Therefore, it was sent to the provincial capital on the 6th. Chief of Staff Xiao of the 18th Division led all the officers to greet it at the division headquarters, set up an altar for mourning, and reported to Minister He and Commander-in-Chief Lu, and notified Zhang's family. Lu, upon hearing the news at the Nanchang Hospital, cried bitterly and was finally persuaded to rest by the doctor. Minister He telegraphed the central government about Zhang's martyrdom and requested compensation. The headquarters of the 18th Division established a mourning hall for Commander Zhang of the 18th Division to handle the funeral arrangements. The office issued a notice yesterday stating, "Respectfully announcing that Army 18th Division Commander Zhang Huizan died unyielding on January 28th in the Futian area, his remains have been brought to the provincial capital, and the coffin will be sealed at 12:00 noon on February 9th at the division headquarters." Zhang's limbs have not been recovered, so a wooden body has been made and joined with his head, dressed in a general's yellow woolen uniform, and placed in a camphor wood coffin worth over 1,000 yuan. Personnel below He and Lu personally mourned at the coffin. The entire 18th Division wore mourning attire and paid respects at the division headquarters, gazing upon the deceased's appearance, all with extraordinary grief. The provincial government has decided to allocate funds for the funeral, and various sectors will also launch a memorial service to express their condolences. (February 9th)

He Yingqin's Admonition to the Bandit Suppression Army

Nanchang Dispatch: He Yingqin recently came to the province to actively plan for bandit suppression. Yesterday, the 5th, in the name of General Commander Chiang, he telegraphed the bandit suppression armies of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian provinces, urging them to abide by it uniformly to facilitate military operations and preserve the reputation of the military. The telegram read, "Protecting the people is the natural duty of soldiers. Disciplining the ranks is the key to victory. The scourge of the communists is not easily defeated, and there are a few troops who do not observe discipline, resulting in the loss of public trust. Consequently, people fear the army and favor bandits, the danger is simply indescribable. I hereby list six items that you must order your subordinates to comply with: (1) Exert every effort to protect the people, and from now on, there shall be no rude or impolite behavior. (2) Do not forcibly take a single blade of grass or tree from the people, nor forcibly conscript laborers or levy grain. (3) Strictly prohibit the protection of opium and gambling. (4) For checkpoints and inspection stations set up by various units, officers should be sent to supervise the inspection of passing luggage, and there must be no deliberate obstruction, detention of innocent people's luggage, or confiscation of money and goods on false pretenses. (5) Except for duty errands, soldiers are strictly prohibited from going out freely. (6) Transportation facilities, such as ships and automobiles, should be specially protected, and no units may arbitrarily detain them without the order of the local senior commander. All my soldiers must know that the people are the lifeline of the army. The above six items must be absolutely obeyed to facilitate the progress of the bandit suppression military and preserve the reputation of the military. If treated as mere formalities, severe punishment will be imposed according to the law. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, He Yingqin acting on his behalf."

He Jian Sends Large Army to Suppress Communist Bandits in Zixing

▲ Departing in Five Routes

Changsha Dispatch: The area around Chaling and Youxian in eastern Hunan, bordering Lianhua, Jinggang, and Ninggang in Jiangxi, has been a place where communist bandits have appeared over the past year. The largest bandit groups are the forces of Chen Shao and Tan Sicong. Chen and Tan are both from Chaling and recently graduated from middle school. They joined the Communist Party in 1924, initially seizing local militias and organizing the Black Killing Squad in Chaling, taking advantage of the policy of suppressing bandits here and fleeing there to launch uprisings. Afterwards, their power grew, and the number of people joining them increased, each having over 1,000 rifles and twice as many personnel. Originally, they were based in Yantang and Yaoshui in Chaling. He Jian, because Chaling and Youxian were important gateways to eastern Hunan, personally went to Youxian last month to survey the terrain and build fortresses, and transferred the entire Tao Liu Brigade of the 19th Division and the entire Qi Guangzhao Bandit Suppression Third Detachment, concentrating them in Youxian and Chaling to suppress them in three routes. On the 26th of last month, they broke through the bandit nests of Yantang and Yaoshui. The two bandits Chen and Tan then fled to Lingxian. Lingxian had no troops, and County Magistrate Sun Zeying led over 1,000 local militia members. Unable to resist when the bandits arrived, they abandoned the city and fled. The communist bandits then occupied the county seat of Lingxian on the 30th of last month. Brigade Commander Tao Liu Fei ordered the two regiments of Tang Xin Zhao and Chen Hanxiong to rush to suppress them, and telegraphed Zi Rugui to prepare his regiment in Guidong to block them. Tang's regiment advanced from Chaling along Kengkouchu and Mindu on the 1st, without any contact. By the 3rd, they had pursued and reached Lingxian. When the county seat was recovered, the bandits had already fled to Zixing with their troops the day before. Various agencies and houses in Lingxian County were burned, dozens of people were killed, and losses were heavy. Zixing also had no garrison troops. Only two teams of local defense forces were dispatched from Yongxing and Leiyang counties, together with the Zixing local militia, totaling over 1,000 people, led by Zixing County Magistrate Yang Yu. They repeatedly engaged and blocked the bandits at Xinkeng, Penggong Temple, Zhou Mensi, and the county seat, but all failed and had over 100 rifles seized by the bandits. Unable to withstand the pressure, they abandoned the county seat at 12:00 noon on the 4th and retreated to Dongjiang to await reinforcements. Thus, the county seat of Zixing was occupied by the bandits again at 2:00 PM on the 4th. Zixing is in the hinterland, indicating that the communist bandits have infiltrated from the border into the hinterland. Therefore, He Jian paid great attention to this and urgently dispatched a large army to encircle and suppress them, as follows: (1) Order Tang Xin Zhao's regiment to pursue the bandits from Lingxian to Zixing. (2) Order Chen Hanxiong's regiment to take a shortcut from Chaling Anren to Longhaitang and advance south towards Zixing. (3) Order He Ping's regiment to advance towards Zixing West from Yongxing. (4) Order Hu Xiang's regiment to advance towards Zixing East from Guidong. (5) Order Chen Long, the Hunan South Garrison Commander, to lead twelve local defense teams from Yizhang Doutousi and advance towards Zixing North. (6) Order Duan Heng, the Hunan South Garrison Commander, to station in Chenzhou and command the above corps to suppress them severely along different routes. The total encircling force is over five regiments, to be concentrated before the 7th for a general offensive. The telegrams from various parties reporting the fall of Zixing are recorded below: (Telegram from Zixing County Magistrate Yang Yu) The communist bandits from Lingxian have all fled to Zixing. The Zixing local defense forces engaged the bandits in a fierce battle in the Xinkeng area and were defeated. Together with the Yongxing local defense forces, they engaged the bandits in fierce battles in Penggong Temple, Zhou Mensi, and other places, but were defeated again and again, and retreated to the county seat. The bandits followed and attacked. I immediately went out of the city to reorganize the troops and defend it. The Leiyang local defense forces arrived in the county to join the suppression. After fierce fighting, the county seat was captured by the bandits. I, carrying the official seal, along with the county party committee and all subordinate agencies, retreated to Dongjiang with the Leiyang local defense forces. I beg you to dispatch a large army to suppress them swiftly and rescue the people of Zixing with utmost urgency. Zixing County Magistrate Yang Yu, respectfully submitted, from Dongjiang. (Telegram from Hunan South Garrison Commander Duan Heng) According to reliable reports, in addition to the two gangs of Chen Shao and Tan Sicong, the red bandits who captured Zixing also include the gang of Li Tianqi. Li is from Leiyang, and most of his gang members are from Leiyang and have fled from the Jiangxi border. Recently, communist bandits have been discovered in Feitian, on the border between Hengyang and Leiyang. They lie in ambush at night, and robberies and killings are frequently heard. Communist bandit slogans are also frequently found on the road. I would like to request you to order Brigade Commander Tao to move to Leiyang to suppress and trấn áp them. Duan Heng, respectfully submitted. (Telegram from 19th Division Brigade Commander Tao Liu) I have just received a telegram from Commander Duan stating that the bandits who captured Lingxian fled to Zixing at the end of the day, and the local defense forces were slightly defeated and retreated to the west bank of Dongjiang to await reinforcements. I have ordered Chen Hanxiong's regiment to take a shortcut from Chaling to Zixing in the early morning to suppress them. Tao Liu, respectfully submitted. (February 7th)

Hunan Province Implements Austerity Measures

▲ Reorganizing Revenue and Reducing Expenditures

Changsha Dispatch: Hunan Province, following orders to abolish Likin taxes, suddenly lost 600,000 yuan in monthly revenue. Zhang Kailian, the Director of the Department of Finance, felt constrained and personally went to Beijing last month to present everything to Chairman Chiang, Minister Song, and others, and requested assistance. In the end, the central government subsidized Hunan Province with 200,000 yuan in political expenses each month. After Director Zhang returned to Hunan, he planned overall. Hunan Province's political expenses required 1,030,000 yuan per month, while under revenue items, (1) the central government subsidized 200,000 yuan, (2) the business tax could collect 100,000 yuan per month, (3) regular and miscellaneous taxes could collect 100,000 yuan per month, (4) the land tax could collect over 200,000 yuan per month, totaling 600,000 yuan per month. There was a difference of over 400,000 yuan between revenue and expenditure, and it would be impossible to maintain without implementing austerity policies. Therefore, a plan for austerity was drafted and submitted to He Jian for approval. The measures were divided into two categories: reorganizing revenue and reducing expenditures. According to Zhang Kailian, if implemented in this way, Hunan's finances could barely cope. The measures are recorded as follows: Measures to Reorganize Revenue (1) All fines from county governments and public security bureaus, water police teams, grain inspection offices, etc., should be included as regular income, and not be concealed, encroached upon, or disposed of by the agencies themselves. (2) The revenue from party dues and party flowers should be temporarily retained to offset party expenses. (3) All judicial revenue at all levels should be retained in full to offset judicial expenses and not be remitted to the central government. (4) All surplus profits from official businesses and mine taxes remitted to the central government should be temporarily retained in full for treasury allocation. (5) Each school's tuition fees and product income should be deducted and remitted by the Department of Finance according to the originally listed budget amount. (6) Reorganize the business income and highway donations of the Highway Bureau and use them as engineering costs for the road bureau, and the provincial treasury will not subsidize them for the time being. (7) For provincial funds received by each county, except for land tax, tooth tax, and various fines, which can be used locally, the remaining deed tax, slaughter tax, and boat donations should all be remitted to the treasury for special projects and not be used locally arbitrarily. (8) The Department of Construction has a large amount of inventory of Cili realgar, Xiangtan tin sand, and Shuikoushan black and white aluminum sand. They should be quickly converted into cash and handed over to the treasury to facilitate turnover.

Measures to Reduce Expenditures (1) Except for revenue collection agencies and agencies with originally listed budget amounts of less than 200 yuan, the office expenses of all agencies shall be issued at 80% of the original amount. (2) Each competent official shall be responsible for removing superfluous personnel from each agency, breaking away from personal feelings, and truly streamlining them. In addition, agencies under their jurisdiction that are superfluous or consume resources, as well as agencies for non-urgent projects, should be truly merged by the competent officials, and the names of the dismissed personnel and agencies should be reported to the provincial government for approval and implementation. (3) No additional expenses shall be added for any item of expenditure that is not listed in the budget. (4) For all construction and repairs and additions exceeding 500 yuan, regardless of whether they have been listed in the budget or not, except for materials and equipment fees for projects that have been completed, contracted, or should be stopped, no requests for payment shall be made on any pretext. (5) For all temporary expenses listed in the budget or approved, the Finance Department Review Committee may suspend payment if it believes that payment can be delayed or that the expenditure is uneconomical. (6) No military temporary expenses shall be diverted or allocated from provincial funds from each county in the future. (7) The expenditures of any agency shall be requested from the provincial treasury and shall not be diverted or allocated from each county. (8) For all education expenses, except for the salt tax surcharge and tuition fees and product income, which are fully used to offset expenses, if there is a shortfall, the competent agency shall evaluate and reduce non-urgent items to ensure suitability, and the treasury will not temporarily compensate for it. (9) Projects that have been listed in the budget or decided to be newly added, but are considered to be delayed, shall not be established for the time being. (10) For expenses that have not been listed in the budget in the future, each competent agency shall deliberate and reject them and shall not arbitrarily propose additional ones. (11) Special expenses of each agency shall be suspended. (12) The expenditures of each government-operated agency shall be truly reduced by the competent agency in conjunction with the financial department. (13) The Minsheng Factory has a huge investment, and it should be started as soon as possible. The expenses shall be paid from the proceeds of the sale of goods. In addition, the official paper printing bureau and the disabled veterans' factory have had tens of thousands of yuan of funds allocated from the provincial treasury. Once the machinery is stopped, it will inevitably rust. The competent agency shall find a way to auction it or solicit merchants to lease it. (14) For bank funds that have been appropriated for military expenses, the loans should be recovered, and the mineral sand stored in the Construction Department should be converted into cash and returned. Business should be started immediately, and corner notes should be issued to facilitate turnover. (February 8th)

Han Fuqu Completes Streamlining

▲ Total of Four Divisions, Three Artillery Regiments, and One Independent Brigade

Jinan Dispatch: Han Fuqu's Third Route Army originally had Sun Tongxuan's 20th Division, Cao Fulin's 29th Division (each division with three brigades, each brigade with three regiments), Gu Liangmin's 22nd Division, Zhan Shutang's 73rd Division, Qiao Lizhi's 74th Division (each division with two brigades, each brigade with two regiments), and Lei Taiping's pistol brigade. In addition, the 20th Division also had Li Xuande's mortar regiment and Sun Shulin's artillery regiment, and the 29th Division also had Wang Yuzhang's artillery regiment, totaling five divisions, one independent brigade, and three artillery regiments. Before the new year, they were ordered to streamline. Sun Tongxuan and Cao Fulin's two divisions were reorganized into Category A divisions, and Gu Liangmin's division was a Category B division, with the division commander numbers remaining the same. Zhan Shutang's division was reorganized into the 58th Brigade of the 20th Division, and Qiao Lizhi's division was reorganized into the 86th Brigade of the 29th Division. However, Han believed that there were too many artillery pieces, and there were no artillery regiments in the new organizational system, so he requested approval from the central government to keep the three artillery regiments of Sun Shulin, Li Xuande, and Wang Yuzhang. However, because there were still too many surplus officers and it was difficult to place them, he requested approval from the central government to reorganize Qiao Lizhi's 86th Brigade into the 74th Division, according to the Category C division organizational system, with Qiao as the division commander. The two brigade commanders will be selected from the three regimental commanders of that brigade: Ma, Fu, and Zeng Chen Zhaoxin. Gu Liangmin's 22nd Division is a Category B division, with two brigades per division and three regiments per brigade. Therefore, the two regiments of Li Yizhi's 66th Brigade were merged into Tang Yaoxun's 65th Brigade, and Li was transferred to be the commander of the 86th Brigade of the 29th Division, formed by selecting one regiment each from the 85th and 87th Brigades of that division. Currently, both Qiao and Li have gone to Beijing for training. After returning to Jinan, they will begin streamlining. Lei Taiping's pistol brigade is directly under the provincial government, and the salaries of the former two Shandong garrison brigades will be transferred to the brigade's salaries. Han's Third Route Army has now completed streamlining, with a total of two Category A divisions, one Category B division, one Category C division, three artillery regiments, and one pistol brigade directly under the provincial government. The division and brigade numbers and the names of the commanders are recorded as follows: (1) 29th Division, Commander Cao Fulin, 85th Brigade Commander Li Hanzhang, 86th Brigade Commander Li Yizhi, 87th Brigade Commander Rong Guangxing, Artillery Regiment Commander Wang Yuzhang. (2) 20th Division, Commander Sun Tongxuan, 58th Brigade Commander Zhan Shutang, 59th Brigade Commander Zhao Xinde, 60th Brigade Commander Ma Jingong, Mortar Regiment Commander Li Xuande, Artillery Regiment Commander Sun Shulin. (3) 22nd Division, Commander Gu Liangmin, 64th Brigade Commander Ning Chunxiao, 65th Brigade Commander Tang Yaoxun. (4) 74th Division Commander Qiao Lizhi. (5) Pistol Brigade Commander Lei Taiping, 1st Regiment Commander Jia Benjia, 2nd Regiment Commander Wu Huawen. (6th)

Min Qian Yuguang's Troops Rebel and Capture Ningde

Fuzhou Dispatch: The Yu and Zhuo companies under Qian Yuguang's troops rebelled and fled from Guping to the Huotong area under Ningde County's jurisdiction, pressing on the county seat. The provincial government received a telegram from Chen Huisheng, the guerrilla captain of Guping, and immediately telegraphed Zhou's Battalion of the First Land Brigade stationed in Gutian to Ningde for reinforcement. However, before Zhou's Battalion arrived, the county seat of Ningde was captured on the 3rd of this month, with widespread looting. However, the rebel soldiers, hearing that reinforcements were coming, retreated to the Shitou area that night and regrouped various bandit gangs, hoping to make another attempt. The reinforcement troops sent by the province have been rushing there day and night. Furthermore, the Ningde Chamber of Commerce also sent a telegram to the province yesterday reporting the situation, which read as follows: "The bandits captured Ningde on [day] and looted extensively. The bandits have temporarily retreated to a place thirty miles from the city. It is learned that the reinforcements are not many and are still gathering various bandit gangs to make another attempt. The whole city is in danger. Please order a large force to rush to support." According to a certain source, after the rebel soldiers of Qian's troops invaded Ningde County, they originally planned to attack the county government, but because there was still a shed of soldiers stationed in the county government, they were unable to succeed. In addition, the troops stationed in Qidu rushed to the scene overnight upon hearing the alarm, so they automatically retreated to the Shitou area. In this battle, 13 bandits were killed and 6 garrison troops died. The area around the east gate was particularly ravaged. (6th)

Zhejiang Provincial Government's Large Loans

▲ 5.5 Million Loan in Shanghai

▲ 1.5 Million Loan in Hangzhou

In order to repay the power plant bonds and raise funds for the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway loan, the Zhejiang Provincial Government sent Director Wang of the Department of Finance to Shanghai to borrow 5.5 million yuan from the Shanghai banking group using the Hangzhou power plant as collateral. The process is as follows: (1) Banking Group Organization: The group was launched due to the large amount of the loan, and was jointly organized and funded by nine banks in Shanghai, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Industrial Bank of China, China Development Bank, Yanye Commercial Bank, etc. It also appointed seven people as directors, including Zhang Zaiyang, Li Fusun, Hu Bijian, Jin Runquan, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhuzhai, and Shen Weizhen, with Zhang as the chairman. It is said that it is named the Hangzhou Power Plant Shanghai Banking Loan Group, but the office is located in Hangzhou. Its functions are to manage the reforms of the factory, supervise the profits and losses of the factory. The group has one secretary and several staff members to handle paperwork. The position of accountant is very important and will be carefully selected and assigned. After the loan is established and managed by the banking group, the factory director and section chiefs will be retained to achieve familiarity and efficiency. The banking group is expected to start work around the end of February. (2) Loan Amount: This loan was negotiated by Director Wang of the Department of Finance in Shanghai with the Shanghai Banking Group with the help of Wang Xiaolai, the chairman of the Shanghai Special Municipality Chamber of Commerce. The amount is 5.5 million yuan. The two sides have contacted and there are already some signs. The content is that the Hangzhou Power Plant is transferred to the banking group for management, and the accumulated profits of the factory over the years are used as interest. It is also heard that the banking group is granted a 30-year patent. After the contract is signed, the profits and losses of the factory's business will have nothing to do with the government. The loan will be paid in six installments, with one installment every 15 days, to be paid off in three months. The formal contract will be signed when the first installment is paid.

Another report: Because the provincial treasury is extremely tight and the funds are owed and urgently needed for distribution, the Department of Finance has negotiated with the banking sector for a loan of 2 million yuan several times. As a result, the banking sector decided to lend 1.5 million yuan. The contract was signed yesterday (9th), with an interest rate of one cent, for a term of six months. The Department of Finance will still use the 2.2 million yuan in foil taxes from the entire province as collateral. Of the 1.5 million yuan loan, 250,000 yuan must be deducted for the previous loan from the Daguan Consolidated Donation. The net current payment is 1.25 million yuan. It was also decided through consultation that the banks and money shops would allocate funds as follows: Bank of China will take on 300,000 yuan, local banks 150,000 yuan, and the remaining 800,000 yuan will be allocated by nine banks, including the Bank of Communications, Deyiye Bank, Industrial Bank of China, China Development Bank, Yanye Commercial Bank, Savings Bank, Chufeng Bank, Huidi Bank, Dalu Bank, etc. The remaining 400,000 yuan will be allocated by the major peers of various money shops. The funds are scheduled to be collected by the 10th and transferred to the Bank of China for transfer to the Department of Finance for verification and collection. (10th)

Northeast First Fleet Commander Ling Xiao Talks About the Current Situation of Weihaiwei

▲ Reasons for the Cold Market in Weihaiwei

▲ Berthing Situation of Northeast Navy Ships

Harbin Dispatch: Ling Xiao, the commander of the Northeast Navy First Fleet stationed in Qingdao, came to Harbin on the afternoon of the 3rd from Shenyang. His visit was to attend the funeral of Shen Honglie, the commander of the Northeast Navy, which was held in Liaoning on the 29th of last month. There are many acquaintances in Harbin, and quite a few people took time to meet him. I visited him at Room 81 on the third floor of the New World Hotel on the afternoon of the 4th and asked him about the current situation of Weihaiwei and the Northeast Navy. According to his account, since the takeover of Weihaiwei, the commercial market has been deserted and not as good as before. During the British management era, Weihaiwei was used as a free trade port, and no customs duties were collected. The local products of various cities and towns along the coasts of Shandong and Jiangsu were mostly transported by sailboats to Weihaiwei for concentration, so the commerce there was developed. After our side took over, customs duties were levied. Originally, Weihaiwei was located between the three major ports of Dalian, Qingdao, and Zhifu, and there was no railway to connect it, so it had no competitive qualifications in principle. Once customs duties were levied, the local products along the coasts of Shandong and Jiangsu mostly shifted to other ports to seek better sales. The commerce of Weihai Port became sluggish. A month ago, local merchants petitioned the National Government to reduce or exempt customs duties. The central government, constrained by treaties, found it difficult to grant a single exemption and did not approve it. The naval authorities intended to develop it as a naval port, which could slightly revitalize commerce, but it would require tens of millions of funds to do so. Therefore, there is no way to save the current decline of Weihaiwei. In reality, Weihaiwei has several disadvantages compared to Jiaozhou Bay: (1) There is no railway connection, so berthing warships will feel a lack of supplies and difficulty in obtaining fuel. (2) There are winds and waves in the port in winter, and only one corner of Liugong Island can avoid the wind. (3) The water in the port is shallow, and the large ships are often attacked by wind and waves, making them unstable. If it is Jiaozhou Bay, large ships can be berthed on both the north and south banks of Qingdao. In the hot summer, the ships can be berthed on the north bank, and in the cold winter, they can be berthed on the south bank. Therefore, foreign ships often come to Jiaozhou Bay in summer to escape the heat (currently, no foreign ships are berthed). As for the Northeast Navy, since the reorganization has not been completed last year, it is still directly under the Northeast and has little direct relationship with the Navy Department. All the salaries are also not assisted by the central government. In the first quarter of 1929, I was ordered to go to Nanjing to participate in the naval reorganization meeting. Although it was an opportunity for the Northeast Navy to approach the central government, I returned because the methods had not been thoroughly negotiated. The First Fleet currently has six warships, all berthed in Qingdao. It does not undertake maritime defense duties. Sometimes, when it goes out on patrol, it also sends out all the ships. Among the ships, the Zhahe is younger, and the Haiqi is older. The headquarters of the First Fleet is located in Qingdao. The naval officers on each ship guide each other in academic studies and cut and polish each other. There is no special school for training. The headquarters of the Second Fleet is stationed in the Changshan Islands, with four gunboats, specializing in maritime patrol and defense. For the convenience of patrol, the north and south banks of Chengjiao Mountain have been divided into two sections, each patrolled by two ships. Huludao and Weihaiwei are patrolled by these two ships. Maritime defense cannot be as clearly divided as land routes. The First Fleet acts as a whole, while the Second Fleet operates in shifts. (4th)

Summary of Jiangsu Province Relief Meeting

The Jiangsu Province Relief Committee held its twelfth meeting on February 5th in the Civil Affairs Department Director's Office. Committee members Wang Zhencheng, Jingsheng, Lu Xiaobo, Chen Qicai (Lin Shaoquan substituting for He Yushu), and Qi Lunjie (substituting for Hu Pu'an) were present. Hu Pu'an chaired the meeting. The following items were discussed: (1) A case regarding how to allocate relief funds due to the heavy disaster reported by Suqian, Siyang, Yancheng, Funing, and other counties, requesting a public decision. Resolution: 1. The 30,000 yuan allocated by the Relief Committee and the 20,000 yuan raised by the Finance Department will be combined for distribution. 2. Allocate 10,000 yuan to Suqian, 10,000 yuan to Siyang, 10,000 yuan to Yancheng, 5,000 yuan to Funing, 4,500 yuan to Rugao, 4,500 yuan to Taixing, 1,000 yuan to Xiaoxian, 1,000 yuan to Jurong, 2,000 yuan to Tongshan, and 2,000 yuan to the Zhenjiang porridge kitchen. 3. The relief funds for Suqian, Siyang, Yancheng, Funing, Rugao, and Taixing counties will be distributed by the Temporary Charity Relief Association. The relief funds for Xiaoxian, Tongshan, Jurong, and Zhenjiang counties will be distributed after each county submits a proposed distribution plan for review and approval. (2) A case from the Nanjing Branch of the Buddhist Swastika Society requesting 1,000 yuan in relief funds for porridge kitchens to provide assistance, requesting a public decision. Resolution: There are no remaining relief funds currently allocated, so it will be discussed after more funds are raised. (3) Committee member Hu Pu'an proposed that the Temporary Charity Relief Association should report the distribution of relief funds to the Provincial Relief Committee for verification.

Page 10

Resolution: 1. The original plan is approved. 2. In the future, the Provincial Relief Committee will additionally hire personnel for the Charity Relief Association to distribute relief funds. (4) Committee member Hu Pu'an proposed that, since Committee member Ye of the Provincial Party Department resigned early, should the Provincial Party Department be requested to appoint another member? Resolution: The Provincial Party Department will be requested to appoint another member. (5) It was resolved to compile and print a collection of relief efforts in the province (from the establishment of the committee to the end of June of the 20th year), with Lin Wenqin, the chief of the document section, responsible for the editing.

Police Investigator Arrives in Songjiang: Gao Tianxu, a police investigator recently appointed by the Civil Affairs Department, arrived in Songjiang on the 9th to investigate various police facilities. He carried several forms to be filled out and verified.

The Provincial Bureau has now appointed Huang Baozhen as the tax collection supervisor, holding a provincial order to take over all official duties of the Public Sales Bureau. Suzhou

Wang Caiyun Loan Case Opens in Court: Wang Caiyun, a 27-year-old woman from Anhui residing at No. 344, North Lane of the Old Gate Bridge in the Shanghai British Concession, sang Suzhou ballads at the Tianyun Building of the Wing On Company. She met Yin Xianfu, who resided at No. 2 opposite the Baiyun Temple on Linyin Road in the South City, in the 7th month of the lunar calendar in 1928. Yin, under the pretense of needing urgent funds for business, borrowed 2,000 yuan from Wang Caiyun, promising to pay interest at 1.8% per month and repay both principal and interest by the end of the lunar year 1929. Yin personally wrote the IOU, but failed to repay the loan by last year. Wang Caiyun repeatedly demanded repayment but was ignored. On July 6th of last year, Wang Caiyun hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit in the Shanghai District Court to recover the loan. After the trial concluded, the court ruled that Yin Xianfu should repay the loan in full. Yin, dissatisfied with the first instance judgment, hired lawyer Ni to appeal to the High Court. Yesterday (the 10th) at 2:00 PM, Judge Mo of the First Civil Division opened the court to hear the appeal. The appellant, Yin Xianfu, did not attend and was represented by lawyer Ni. The appellee, Wang Caiyun, personally appeared in court with lawyers Lin and Zhao. Wang Caiyun eloquently described the events. Lawyer Ni presented evidence in court that Wang Caiyun had already received the repayment and presented a fingerprint receipt. Judge Mo ordered the lawyers for both parties to argue and adjourned the court, setting the judgment for the 14th of this month.

Wang Xinyu's Speculation Failure, Continued: Wang Xinyu, the manager of the Qianfeng South Goods Store at Duting Bridge, engaged in gold standard speculation in Shanghai and failed, involving the store and various banks and money shops that had dealings with the store. Representatives from each bank and money shop arrived at the store the night before to audit the accounts and inventory. It is now learned that after the representatives audited the accounts, they believed that the store had a significant amount of outstanding loans and could be maintained. Furthermore, since the store was an old establishment of over 60 years, the shareholders were reluctant to order it to close down immediately. Therefore, the store continues to operate as usual. A representative has been sent to Shanghai to find Wang Xinyu and bring him back to Suzhou to handle the situation. However, as of yesterday, there was still no news of Wang Xinyu's return. It is rumored that Wang Xinyu's speculation losses amount to 180,000 yuan.

County Chamber of Commerce Appeals on Behalf of Private Postal Services: Due to Article 5 of the Postal Bureau's regulations for banning private postal services, which requires private postal services to have their mail weighed and forwarded by the post office, the private postal service industry in Wu County believes that it is difficult to comply. They have sent a letter to the Wu County Chamber of Commerce for assistance. The County Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Transportation on the 10th, requesting amendments to protect the livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of merchants and workers in the private postal service industry.

Little Monk Kong Sentenced to Seven Death Penalties: The notorious bandit Little Monk Kong of Taihu Lake (also known as Kong Xiangfa) has committed numerous major cases of kidnapping, robbery, and murder in Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Chengxiang. After the water police arrested the criminal, the Wu County District Court sentenced him to seven death penalties on the 9th.

Kunshan

Change of Personnel in the Kunshan Detective Team: Captain Wang of the local detective team has resigned due to personal reasons. Wu Shaokang, a supervisor from the Public Security Bureau, has been promoted to fill the vacancy and has already taken office.

Wuxi

Representatives of Various County Chambers of Commerce Schedule a Meeting: When Jiangsu Province organized the collection of business tax registration fees last year, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce convened representatives from various county chambers of commerce in Zhenjiang and established a temporary joint office to achieve mutual assistance. The Jiangsu Provincial Government believes that the government has implemented the business tax and the implementation period has arrived. The formulated tax regulations not only exceed the ministry's guidelines, but the tax rates set in Jiangsu Province are also higher than those set in Zhejiang and Anhui provinces. They have jointly contacted the chambers of commerce of various counties and sent telegrams to the ministry and province, requesting detailed review and revision. Since the National Government and the ministry have not yet issued clear instructions, the local chambers of commerce have repeatedly requested that the provincial chamber of commerce hold another meeting to decide on a solution. It has been scheduled to meet in Zhenjiang on February 25th. A comparative table of various tax rates has been prepared and opinions are being sought from local chambers of commerce to be presented for discussion at the meeting.

Heavy Snow Affects Commerce: After spring began, the weather in Wuxi turned warm until the night of August 8th, when heavy rain began and continued until 1:00 PM on the 9th, followed by heavy snow. It stopped snowing on the morning of yesterday. The snow accumulated to over one foot. Many city and rural electric light and telephone poles and lines were crushed by the snow. Over 300 telephone lines within and outside the city were out of service, and over 40 rural telephone lines were out of service. It was also reported that long-distance telephone lines to Beijing and Shanghai were also interrupted. At a time when merchants are preparing to close their accounts, business operations and accounts have been greatly affected.

Shenjiawan Robbery Reported and Under Investigation: Zhang Qingchen, the village head of District 396 of Nanyan City in the county, lives in Shenjiawan. At around 10:00 PM the night before, over 20 bandits, all speaking with a Jiangbei accent, broke open the back door and rushed in. They first tied up Zhang Qingchen with ropes, forced him to reveal the location of the silver, and carried out a major robbery, stealing over 100 yuan in clothing and silver.

Two Fires Result in Three Deaths: In the fifth district of the county, the home of Shen Xijiu, a wealthy resident of Chentang near Shitou Town, was using a stove for warmth recently because the weather has been very cold. On the night of the 8th, at a little after 1:00 AM, the coal ashes poured out of the stove were not completely extinguished, and the fire spread, piercing through the roof. At that time, the entire Shen family was sound asleep. Later, Shen Xijiu's wife, Liu, noticed and woke up the family members. Unfortunately, one nephew was unable to be carried out from his bed. Liu returned to the room to carry out her nephew, but both were caught in the fire and were buried in the flames. The next morning, Shen Xijiu hired workers to dig out the bodies, which were like charred wood. The scene was very tragic. Also, at the home of Jiang Axu, a resident of Jiangxiangshang near Qianzhou in the fifteenth district, a fire broke out suddenly at a little after 12:00 AM the night before. Fortunately, firefighters from the town arrived and were able to extinguish the fire, but the house they lived in was completely destroyed. After the fire broke out, Axu's mother, who was 77 years old, was unable to walk due to her advanced age and also died in the fire.

New World Hotel Caught Stealing Electricity: The Qishuyan Power Plant's office in Wuxi has recently discovered that many electricity users are stealing electricity, and has organized an inspection team and sent out many inspectors to investigate. In recent days, many electricity users have been caught stealing electricity. At 10:00 PM the night before, inspectors discovered that the seal on the electric meter box of the New World Hotel under the Gongyun Bridge outside Guangfu Gate had been moved, and there was a piece of iron wire in the electric meter box. The inspectors immediately questioned the hotel's accountant, who was evasive. They then took down the electric meter box and reported back to the factory. The factory, upon receiving the report, intends to follow the electricity theft punishment rules promulgated by the Construction Committee, which stipulate that electricity thieves should be charged electricity fees based on the highest electricity usage month in the past year, calculating the electricity consumption for the year as compensation for the loss of stolen electricity. The hotel should compensate between 6,000 and 4,000 yuan. The factory now plans to hire a lawyer to file a complaint with the county court.

Abnormal Plant Growth, Winter Vegetables Bloom: The weather in the county last winter was unusually warm and cold, causing summer weather to occur in winter, with three thunderstorms. The last two occurred in late January, when the weather was unusually warm, like the third month of the lunar calendar. This led to the outbreak of an epidemic in the market. According to elderly farmers, winter thunder is the omen of misfortune. The recent epidemic in the market confirms this belief. Recently, winter vegetables planted in the county's fields have suddenly bloomed. According to elderly farmers, this is also an omen of misfortune. This is recorded for plant scientists to study.

Changzhou

Reformatory Decided to Expand: The Wujin County Government previously convened a countywide administrative meeting and decided to expand the reformatory to accommodate more vagrants, due to the increasing number of vagrants in the area. After County Magistrate Zhang took office, he proposed the expansion for discussion at the county administration meeting on the 9th. It was decided to implement the expansion measures: (1) Temporary expansion expenses will be advanced by the Finance and Property Department. (2) The recurring expansion expenses will be based on the number of increased inmates starting from March of this year. The director of the reformatory will create a table at the end of each month showing the actual number of inmates and the required expenses, and submit it to the county government for transfer to the Finance and Property Department for advancement. (3) All temporary and recurring advances will be listed in the budget for the 20th year. (4) The vagrants added to the reformatory will be limited to those transferred by the county government or the bandit suppression bureau, with a maximum of 60 people. Vagrants sent by the district offices will still be handled as usual.

Changshu

True or False: The Maojia Bridge Robbery and Kidnapping Case: The Shen Tongshun oil mill in Maojia Bridge outside the North Gate of this county was robbed on the 16th of last month, and the manager Yao Shou and employee Xue Guanxing were kidnapped. After County Magistrate Tan and Public Security Bureau Chief Wang visited the area for an on-site investigation the next day, the county ordered the case to be solved within five days. However, before a few days had passed, Yao and Xue suddenly returned, claiming that the bandits had released them unconditionally. Everyone who heard this believed it to be true. However, recently, society has been abuzz with discussions claiming that Yao Shou embezzled a large sum of money from the oil mill and was unable to make up for it, so he faked the robbery in an attempt to shut down the business. There are six points of suspicion in this case: (1) The neighbors on either side did not hear anything on the night of the robbery and kidnapping. (2) When the county bureau chief and others went to the area for an on-site inspection, Yao's wife replied that she did not know anything. (3) It is said that the robbers came from and left through Gengjingkou, where water police and police teams are stationed, so they should not have been completely unaware. (4) According to the account, there were only two or three guns among the robbers, so how dare they rob in a place only three or four miles away from the city? (5) Since Yao Shou was kidnapped, why was he released unconditionally? (6) Since Yao and others were released, why do they always avoid appearing in public? The above six points are indeed very suspicious. Now, various creditor groups have heard the news and are rushing to demand payment. The authorities will also conduct a thorough investigation to uncover the truth.

Five Counties Jointly Suppress Pirates: The five counties of Tong, Ru, Hai, Qi, and Chang have recently decided to dispatch teams to jointly suppress pirates due to pirate disturbances. Police ships from each county and patrol boats from the Provincial Water Public Security Team have also joined the blockade. According to telephone reports, most of the pirates in the Yijia Town area have retreated to Linglishan in the Lusi waters.

Relief Center Takes Over Charitable Organizations: The Nantong Relief Center has been established. However, old-age homes, orphanages, and homes for the disabled have refused to be taken over because they were privately donated. On the 9th, the county government ordered the Public Security Bureau to transfer the Qiliu and Jiliang institutions under its jurisdiction to the Relief Center. The charitable assets held by the Finance and Property Department will also be transferred this month.

Counterfeit Money Sellers Arrested: A man surnamed Tang in Hongqiao, at the border of Jiangdu County across the river from Zhenjiang, had been using counterfeit money in Zhenjiang. On the afternoon of the 8th, five men, including one surnamed Zhang, came across the river to demand payment because they had previously sold Tang counterfeit money, selling each 100 yuan of counterfeit money for 30 yuan in real money, owing 700 yuan. They argued and fought, which was discovered by the inspection team of the troops stationed in Liuwei, who learned of the previous situation. Zhang and others were arrested because the matter involved counterfeiting currency, which they could not handle, so they were transferred to Yangzhou for handling yesterday.

Sheng Nage Plots to Kill Wife: Sheng Nage, a 22-year-old farmer from Xinfeng Township, does not engage in honest work and indulges in reckless behavior. Three years ago, he married Guo, who is quite virtuous and is now 21 years old. She has already given birth to a daughter. Guo has repeatedly admonished him, which has caused him to hate her. A few days ago, Nage took advantage of Guo's sleep to insert a pearl needle into Guo's vagina. Guo woke up in excruciating pain. After being interrogated by her, Sheng admitted the truth. Guo then told her aunt-in-law and asked her to treat her, but was refused. Then, Guo told her mother, who came to the city with her and sought treatment at the Christian Hospital. The doctor performed surgery and was fortunately able to remove the needle. Now, Guo and her mother plan to sue in court.

Jiangsu Provincial Relief Committee Allocates Relief Funds: The Jiangsu Provincial Relief Committee held its twelfth meeting yesterday in the Civil Affairs Department and resolved to combine the 30,000 yuan allocated by the Relief Committee and the 20,000 yuan raised by the Finance Department for distribution to various counties: 10,000 yuan to Suqian, 10,000 yuan to Siyang, 10,000 yuan to Yancheng, 5,000 yuan to Funing, 4,500 yuan to Rugao, 4,500 yuan to Taixing, 1,000 yuan to Xiaoxian, 1,000 yuan to Jurong, 2,000 yuan to Tongshan, and 2,000 yuan to the Zhenjiang porridge kitchen. The relief funds for Suqian, Siyang, Yancheng, Funing, Rugao, and Taixing counties will be distributed by the Temporary Charity Relief Association. The relief funds for Xiaoxian, Tongshan, Jurong, and Zhenjiang counties will be distributed after each county submits a proposed distribution plan for review and approval. The subsidy fee for the Nanjing porridge kitchen will be discussed after more funds are raised.

Yangzhou Escapee Arrested in Zhenjiang: Wang Dehua, a notorious criminal who escaped from prison in Yangzhou last year, is 27 years old and from Taihe County, Anhui. After escaping from prison, he joined a gang of bandits to rob a small steamer, then fled to Zhenjiang in secret. Yesterday, Yangzhou detective Liu Pu led police to Zhenjiang to search for him and, together with Detective Wu of the Provincial Public Security Bureau's detective team, arrested the criminal in a bathhouse. They also searched Wang's residence at No. 5, West Lotus Pond, at the entrance of the railway and found a pistol and 65 bullets. The criminal was escorted to Yangzhou for interrogation this morning. Last night, the Seventh Branch of the Provincial Public Security Bureau also sent Wang's landlord, Lin Qingfa, along with the lease agreement to the bureau for questioning.

Jiangyin

Conclusion Method of the Zhou Shuiping Case Announced: The Provincial Party and Government's Fifth Discussion Meeting decided on three methods for the Zhou Shuiping case. After investigating the results, it was reported to the provincial government after a discussion by the review meeting. The 357th meeting resolved to assign Sha Bingyuan and 37 other people to each contribute 2,000 yuan, designating 50,000 yuan as the Zhou Shuiping Memorial Elementary School Fund and 26,000 yuan for tomb repair and pension. After the disposal, those who accused Zhou were exempt from arrest, and his property was unsealed, and letters were sent to the Provincial Party and Government Committee, the High Court, and the Civil Affairs Department to order the Jiangyin County Magistrate to comply and report. After drafting the handling procedure, it was reported to the provincial government for instructions. After the defendants pay the full amount, they will report to the government so that the property can be unsealed and the arrest warrants can be revoked. As for the memorial elementary school, it should be handled by the county magistrate and the Education Bureau. After receiving the order, Magistrate Li believed that after the defendants were wanted, they had all fled to other places with unknown addresses and could not be notified. Therefore, they should be served by public announcement and require the defendants to immediately comply with the resolution disposal measures of the provincial government and each pay 2,000 yuan to the government for separate handling.

Another Robbery Occurs in the City: A robbery occurred at the home of Gui Sheng in Nancangwan in the city, and the case has not yet been solved for a few days. Unexpectedly, on the 8th, Ji Yongbei, a resident of Huashan Township, was robbed in Wenchang Lane in the south of the city. At 9:00 AM, Ji Yongbei went to the county to pay the grain tax and was carrying 16 yuan in silver when he passed through the area. He was suddenly confronted by four bandits who threatened him and robbed him of the silver he was carrying.

Yangzhou

Police Team Escorts Large Batch of Stolen Goods and Bandits: At around 5:00 PM on the 8th, Wang Zhuxiang, the leader of the third squad of the first squadron of the police stationed in Yiling, escorted 17 male and female bandits (4 men, 5 women, and 8 children) and over 100 pieces of stolen goods and luggage to the city. Han, the squadron leader, immediately handed them over to the detective team for custody and preliminary investigation. It was learned that the bandits were reported by an informant to be residing at the home of Wang Xiaolai in Xuejia, Yiling, who had many male and female bandits speaking with a dialect from south of the river. Wang, the squad leader, dispatched plainclothes police with weapons to investigate. They found four or five men and women at Wang's house. When the police arrived, the women blocked the door, and the men entered the house and escaped over the wall. The police opened fire to pursue them and captured Xu Chunnian and Wang San on the spot. They then searched Wang's house and found stolen goods. During the preliminary investigation, Xu confessed that he had participated in the robbery of the Dada Yantai steamer at Minhekou on December 12th and did not deny sharing the loot. Meanwhile, squadron leader Han received a telephone report from the squad and dispatched a police team to Yiling overnight to assist in capturing three pirate ships and female bandits and children. The ships contained stolen goods such as peanuts, clothes, and luggage. Han has now submitted a report to the brigade headquarters and the county government for review.

All Schools Resume Classes and Issue Declarations: The elementary schools in Jiangdu have been on strike to demand salaries for four weeks. After the authorities agreed to first pay three months' salaries, classes were resumed on the 9th and a declaration was issued, stating that they could not bear to let the children be without education, so they would resume classes first and find ways to make up for the children's studies. At the same time, they will submit a report to the provincial department, requesting the county bureau to formulate a plan to repay the arrears and maintain the treatment of colleagues, and work with the Party Department to convene a teaching fee clearing committee to start reorganizing to consolidate the foundation of teaching fees.

He arrived at the county government at 8:00 AM on the 8th to take over the seal and assume office.

Elementary School Principals Request Prompt Salary Payments: The teaching fees for all elementary schools in Yangzhong County have only been paid up to the first half of December. Elementary school teachers in general are suffering because the accounting period for the business community is approaching. At the principals' meeting held by the Education Bureau on the 8th (today), the principals of various elementary schools questioned the lack of transparency in the collection and expenditure of teaching fees. Director Wang Huankun stated that the number of county government payments not allocated was still large and ordered the principals to elect representatives to petition the county government. As a result, Magistrate Zhao soothed them, checked the case, allocated funds, and dispersed them.

Jiaxing

Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the County Chamber of Commerce Have Been Elected: The Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce held its inaugural meeting on the 9th. 320 members signed in. After discussing various proposals, they held a secret ballot election. As a result, Yao Zitong, Gao Zhonglan, Shen Xiping, Lu Chujue, Jiang Laixian, Song Jinglian, and 9 others were elected as executive committee members. County Government Mediates Car Rental Dispute: The rickshaw pullers of Jiaxing went on strike due to car rental issues a few days ago. After the authorities persuaded the rickshaw pullers to resume work first, they convened representatives from both sides to hold a meeting for mediation. It is now learned that on the afternoon of the 9th, the Construction Bureau of the County Government specially convened representatives from both labor and management to hold a mediation meeting. After a long period of dispute between the representatives of both sides, County Magistrate Gong mediated a compromise, stating that if it is a daily rental, the daily payment is 4.2 jiao (an increase of 2 jiao according to the regulations). If it is a monthly rental, the daily payment is still 4 jiao. The representatives of the car companies signed on the spot, but the representatives of the rickshaw pullers did not sign. Therefore, it is feared that the mediation will not take effect.

Letters

Letter from the Fourth District Office of Jinshan County

To the Editor: I recently read in the Songjiang Correspondence column of your newspaper on February 4th that "dozens of bandits suddenly came to Ganxiang Town and went to the Public Security Bureau and the District Office, intending to coerce the leaders of each to point out the names of more than 30 wealthy households in the town and demand 12,000 yuan to raise funds. As a result, in addition to robbing police weapons, they also took away a list of wealthy households." This is not entirely consistent with the facts. At that time, the bandits came to the town and wrote five letters of demand, requesting the District Office to forward them, but the assistant sternly refused. As a result, the bandits delivered them directly. The police weapons of the Public Security Bureau were not robbed. Fearing that rumors would be untrue and confuse the public, I have written this letter to state the actual situation and request that it be published in the Letters column for correction. Sincerely, Fourth District Office of Jinshan County.

Education News - Important News

Inaugural Meeting of the Yunnan Provincial Education Association

(Yunnan Correspondent) At 12:00 noon on January 25th, the Provincial Education Association held its inaugural meeting at the former site of the Provincial Education Department in Changchunfang. Those in attendance included Chairman Long, committee members Chen and Chen from the Provincial Party Committee, Education Director Gong Zhongjun, dozens of representatives from various institutions, organizations, and schools, and over 100 county education representatives. The ceremony was conducted in accordance with etiquette. After distributing declarations, Zhao Shuren, the chairman of the preparatory committee, reported on the preparations. Chairman Long then gave instructions, stating that the Provincial Education Association had previously only sought the interests of a few people and its own association. Now that it has been reorganized, it is hoped that it will fulfill its due responsibilities to the country and society. Next, Chen Zhenzhi, a member of the Provincial Steering Committee, gave a speech, stating that Chinese education had previously suffered from two problems: impracticality and a lack of talent, and the transformation of party education into a religious ritual, which was not practical. He hoped that the association would strive to innovate after its establishment. During this period of political tutelage, educational construction is the primary task of political and economic construction, eliminating laxity and cultivating orderly and trained talents. Education officials have a great responsibility and are expected to work hard. Then, Education Director Gong of the Education Department gave a speech, stating that the reorganization and establishment of the association are very different from the past in terms of the way they are produced and the organizational foundation. In the past, it was only organized by a few people from the education community in the provincial capital, and each was equal in form. Now, it is based on the counties and united by the Provincial Education Association. The voice can express a new spirit. In the past, education only focused on senior urban male assets, etc., and in the future, attention should be paid to junior rural female poor people, etc. The province's education plan is planned to be divided into two sections: one section for high schools and above and specialized universities, which can be named higher education, focusing on maintaining and enriching, and temporarily not expanding, so that it can be scientific and modernized, and the European and American systems can be adopted, with the primary goal of creating practical construction talents. One section for junior high schools and below and popular compulsory education can be named national education, focusing on promotion and perfection, so that it can be popularized, and only the Chinese system can be adopted. This is the common goal of our education colleagues. In addition, I hope that everyone will pay more attention to research, investigation, and statistics to supplement the shortcomings of the educational administration agency. Also, the most important thing for the education community in this province to solve now is the teacher issue. The Jiangsu correspondence method is proposed to be imitated, such as the salary issue of primary school teachers, which will be subsidized by the province in the future, and the scholarship fund will also be raised by the government. In short, I hope that educational colleagues will work hard. Then, Representative Yang Tianli replied, saying that he would follow the instructions of the leaders and committee members, and colleagues would promote reform and realization. Then, after tea and snacks, slogans were chanted, photos were taken, and the meeting adjourned. It is reported that the Education Department plans to take advantage of the visit of representatives from various counties to the province to hold a temporary education advisory meeting on the 26th, 27th, and 28th of this month.

Lu Education Administrative Conference Concludes

A quick dispatch from Jinan states that today (the 7th) was the seventh and final day of the Second Shandong Provincial School Education Administrative Conference. The eighth general meeting was held at 9:00 AM, with 34 members in attendance. He Siyuan served as chairman, Liu Cixiao as master of ceremonies, and Yang Peng as recorder. The meeting proceeded according to the agenda: (A) The chairman reverently read the Prime Minister's will; (B) Reports on various matters: (1) Report on the results of the deliberation by the salary standard advisory group for secondary school teachers and staff (report by Pi Songyun). It was resolved that the report be adopted with revisions based on the group's discussion. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM, and it was decided to continue the meeting from 1:00 PM to 3:30 PM to discuss the remaining unresolved cases. The meeting resumed at 1:00 PM, with Lai Zhizhong presiding, beginning with the second case: (2) Report on the results of the deliberation by the group on the curriculum and regulations for rural normal schools (report by Lai Zhizhong). It was resolved that, concerning curriculum-related matters, the original group would continue to refine the details based on the opinions of the general meeting and submit them to the department for approval. Dong Huai, Chen Jianheng, Liu Kunshan, and the director of the primary school attached to the First Rural Normal School were added as reviewers, still convened by Ma Rumei; the rest of the group's deliberation results were adopted with revisions. (3) Report on the results of the deliberation by the group on enhancing the efficiency of primary school education. It was resolved that the department would be notified based on the group's results. The meeting adjourned at 3:30 PM, thus declaring the conclusion of the Second Shandong Provincial Education Administrative Conference. However, no ceremony was held. It is reported that all unfinished matters will be addressed in the Education Department without further meetings. Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, originally planned to attend the closing ceremony but was unable to do so due to an incompletely healed leg ailment. He Siyuan, Director of the Education Department, hosted a banquet for all members at the YMCA at 6:00 PM. Han Fuqu did not attend. The atmosphere was filled with toasts and cheer.

▲Discussion by the Budget Vocational Education Staff Salary Standard Group for the 20th Year: Regarding the salary standard case for vocational education staff in the 20th year budget, the general meeting had previously resolved to refer it to this group for review and drafting. After deliberation by colleagues, the following seven principles are respectfully reported: (1) Restrict concurrent teaching by principals; the method is that principals should not teach more than six hours concurrently, and no additional salary will be paid for exceeding this limit. (2) Teacher remuneration shall be based on a standard of $1.75 per hour for senior high school and $1.25 per hour for junior high school, calculated by credit hours, but each person shall not teach more than 22 hours per week. If it is necessary to exceed this limit, prior approval should be sought from the Department of Education for (1) Chinese language teachers to have additional credit hours for grading papers, and (2) vocational and technical school teachers to have additional credit hours for factory instruction and design. (4) Department heads' salaries shall be increased by $10 compared to the 19th-year budget, and concurrent teaching credit hours shall not exceed ten hours. (5) Librarians, clerks, accountants, and general affairs officers should all be referred to as administrative staff, and their total salaries should be listed without separate listings, so that schools have room for flexibility. (6) The position of Han-level director is abolished, and with the original funding, instructors are appointed as appropriate, but vocational schools with special circumstances may still retain the title of department head. (7) The salary standards for teachers and staff in provincial primary schools shall be increased as appropriate by the Department of Education in accordance with each school's 20th-year plan. (8) Each school's Boy Scout office expenses are $10 per month. (9) Each school principal's office expenses are increased by $10 per month.

Municipal Party Department Prepares to Recommend Party Members for Teaching Positions

▲Registration to be Held for Half a Month Starting from the 15th

▲Party Members with Qualifications as Primary and Secondary School Teachers

▲Whether Employed or Unemployed, All Must Register

The Training Department and Organization Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang jointly issued a notice to the various district branches of the city, stating that as the period of political tutelage begins and everything is waiting to be done, it is a time when the country urgently needs talent and when our party members should strive for construction. Twenty Organizations Host Dr. Carleton Washburne

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, the China Child Education Society, Shanghai University, the Real Sphere, the Chinese Student Association, and other organizations have jointly initiated a gathering of various groups and schools to host the American education expert Dr. Carleton Washburne. As previously reported, the organizations and schools that have joined include the Shen Bao Newspaper, the Xinwen Bao Newspaper, Jiaotong University, Jinan University, Labor University, Fudan University, Daxia University, Guanghua University, Datong University, Sino-French Vocational School, Commercial Press, Chung Hwa Book Company, World Book Company, Kaiming Bookstore, Beixin Bookstore, and the China Children's Welfare Association, totaling twenty organizations. In addition to a public banquet at the Bankers' Association on the 15th, Dr. Washburne has also been specially invited to give ten lectures. Dr. Washburne's brief biography is introduced below:

Dr. Carleton Washburne comes from a scholarly family. His mother was a famous lecturer and the first editor of the Elementary School Education Magazine. His father was a doctor. Therefore, Dr. Washburne benefited greatly from his mother's teaching and was also inspired by his father. In 1912, he graduated from Stanford University. He initially worked for a real estate company, and then entered the education field, serving as a primary school principal, which allowed him to experiment with his individual teaching methods. However, due to a lack of understanding from the education authorities, the experiment was not successful. At this time, Brook, a famous educator who advocated breaking the class teaching system, happened to be the president of the San Francisco State Normal School. After reading Brook's educational thesis, "The Entrenchment of Teaching and Its Remedies," Dr. Washburne resonated with it and began to interact and discuss teaching methods with Brook. As a result, Dr. Washburne became a professor at Brook's normal school in 1914. Subsequently, Brook introduced him to Winnetka to experiment with Dr. Washburne's educational ideals. Thus, Dr. Washburne's individual teaching method became known to the world as the Winnetka Plan.

Wing On Textile Factory Sends Personnel to Japan for Investigation

The Wing On Textile Factory in Yangshupu produces high-quality products and has achieved business success.
