Order Regarding the Organization of People's Associations

The Shanghai County Government issued an instruction to the district chiefs yesterday, stating: To comply with the case, the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department telegraphed: The Provincial Government telegraphed: The National Government forwarded a letter from the Central Association, stating: Three measures are prescribed for the reorganization or re-organization of people's associations within a limited time: (1) The deadline for the reorganization of various people's associations, except for the Farmers' Association, which will be determined after the promulgation of the Farmers' Association Law, and the Chamber of Commerce, which should be handled in accordance with Articles 6 and 7 of the revised Chamber of Commerce Law as resolved by the National Government's State Council, unless otherwise stipulated by laws and regulations, all workers' unions and social organizations must complete their reorganization by the end of January of the 20th year of the Republic of China [1931]. (2) Various people's associations that have passed the statutory deadline for reorganization but have not yet completed the reorganization should be reorganized in accordance with the organizational plan for people's associations and the relevant laws and regulations for each association. (3) Those who re-organize various people's associations must formally organize and establish them before February 15 of the 20th year of the Republic of China [1931], and the Yuan [Executive Yuan] is to instruct its subordinates to comply. In addition to issuing a notice, the Provincial Party Rectification Association and the Civil Affairs and Agriculture and Mining Departments are to be informed separately. You are instructed to order your subordinates to comply and submit a list of associations that have been reorganized or need to be re-organized for review. Upon receiving this, we hereby urgently telegraph the County Magistrate to instruct the various associations under your jurisdiction to quickly instruct them to reorganize or organize separately and complete the reorganization within the specified time. Also, thoroughly investigate and fill out the attached form with the details of associations that have been reorganized or need to be re-organized in the county and submit it for compilation and forwarding. Forms will be issued to the county. Upon receiving this, in addition to investigating and reporting the various associations that have been organized in the form and sending them separately, we hereby instruct the District Chief to follow the instructions and notify the district to separately reorganize or organize in accordance with the regulations and within the specified time, and report back for review without any delay. This order is imperative.

Record of the Joint Association of Guild Halls and Public Offices

▲ Seven Committee Members Appointed

Our city's various guild halls and public offices, having seen the newspaper report that Shanghai Municipal Government Notice No. 215 requires all social organizations and charitable organizations in the city to apply for registration before March 31 in accordance with the central government's promulgated Supervisory Law for Charitable Organizations and the Social Organization Organization Procedures, otherwise they will be strictly dealt with. However, the old organizational structures and original charters of the various guild halls and public offices are largely inconsistent with current laws and regulations, and they are not very clear about the registration procedures, making progress extremely difficult. Therefore, the Joint Association of Guild Halls and Public Offices convened a meeting of its members the day before yesterday. On that day, representatives from more than 30 organizations attended, which was sufficient to meet the legal quorum. Chen Liangyu was publicly elected as chairman, and after the rituals were performed, the chairman announced the purpose of the meeting, stating that the municipal government's deadline for registration was very pressing, and each organization should prepare and proceed as soon as possible, and not delay any further. After lengthy discussions by the representatives, it was decided to publicly elect seven committee members to form a review committee to separately review the original charters of each organization and formulate standard reorganization measures so that the affiliated organizations could follow them in order to proceed with registration separately. Chen Liangyu, Guo Zhongliang, Weng Yaheng, Gao Jianqing, Chen Yiting, Cheng Qingtao, and Wu Shutian were immediately appointed as members of the review committee, and Wu Shutian was publicly elected to be responsible for convening the review meetings at 4 p.m. every Sunday afternoon in order to carry out the review. At the same time, a notice was sent to all affiliated organizations to send their original charters and old organizational overviews to the association within one week for forwarding to the review committee for verification. Those organizations that have already been approved for registration are also requested to send a copy of their charters, etc., for reference.

Procedures for Resignation and Replacement of Committee Members of Trade Associations

▲ Vacancies Can Be Filled by Substitute Committee Members According to Law

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a notice to all trade associations, stating: We respectfully inform you that on September 12 of last year, we received a letter from the Cotton Cloth Trade Association stating that Articles 14 and 24 of the association's charter stipulate that the resignation or retirement of committee members must be approved by a general meeting of members. However, among the elected executive committee members of this session, some are determined to resign, leading to the following questions: (1) Does the provision in the charter specifically refer to committee members after they have taken office, so that once elected, they are all bound by it? (2) The general meeting of members is held once a year according to the charter. Before the meeting is convened and passed, should the resignation of the committee member be put on hold, or should it be considered an urgent issue that requires a special meeting to be convened? If it is difficult to convene a meeting, or the quorum is not met, what remedy is available? Please provide instructions. After deliberation at the 12th regular meeting of our Chamber, it was decided that the resignation or retirement of elected personnel, regardless of whether it is stated in the charter, must be approved by the original election body according to the source of authority. However, these meetings are often difficult to convene. Therefore, as a general practice, unless the number of resigning personnel is excessive, requiring a general meeting to be convened to resolve the issue in accordance with the law, if only a small number of people apply for resignation after being elected, the majority of the elected personnel can take office first and then convene a meeting to discuss whether to approve the resignation. If the resignation is approved, the substitute member should be notified to fill the vacancy, and a report should be submitted to the competent authorities for record. This situation was communicated to the Cotton Cloth Trade Association, and the proposed measures were submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval. On the 6th of this month, we received Instruction No. 5859 from the Social Affairs Bureau, which stated: Regarding the case submitted by the Association, concerning the method of deciding whether the power to approve or disapprove the resignation of elected officials of trade associations should be decided, the case has been reviewed and approved. It has been reported to the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and Instruction No. 13607 stated: It has been found that there are clear provisions on the approval of resignations of officials of various associations, and the various measures proposed by the Association are appropriate and should be notified for compliance. However, the Association's original proposed measures included a clause on notifying substitute members to fill vacancies. The method of generating these substitute members was not specified in detail. The Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law also does not have any explicit provisions. The case was submitted to the Ministry of Industry for review. Instruction No. 389 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stated: The report has been received. It has been found that the method of generating substitute executive committee members of the association can be determined in accordance with Article 16 of the Implementing Rules of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, which can be used as a reference for the provisions of Article 15 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law, i.e., when the association elects executive committee members, it may elect substitute committee members separately, who will fill vacancies in order. As for the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce's reply that the provisions on industry associations were not applicable to the Chamber of Commerce, this refers to Article 11 of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, which clearly stipulates the retirement of officials, and cannot be used as a reference for Article 22, Paragraph 3 of the Chamber of Commerce Law. It is not the case that any provisions for which there are no other regulations cannot be used as a reference for the Chamber of Commerce Law. Although Article 9 of the Association Law does not stipulate the title of substitute committee members, it is consistent with the meaning of the separate rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law. In order to facilitate the actual situation, if the association's charter stipulates the substitute committee members by itself, it is not inconsistent with the law. Based on the information presented, you are hereby notified. As the Association's proposed method of notifying substitute members to fill vacancies was submitted to the Ministry of Industry for review, it is hereby ordered that the Association be notified and that all affiliated trade associations be notified for compliance. The various labor unions often interpret the Chamber of Commerce Law on the grounds that the Association Law does not have any provisions for substitute executive committee members, and there are limitations on the application of the Chamber of Commerce Law, which causes difficulties in implementation. As a result of the aforementioned, each industry can now handle matters in accordance with these regulations. A letter is hereby issued for notification, hoping that you will all act accordingly.

Reference for Export Trade to France

▲ The Industrial and Commercial Visitation Bureau Has a Graphic Index

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce received an instruction from the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: To inform the prefect, a communication was received from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating: The Consul General in Paris has reported that he has recently received letters from our merchants in Shanghai or Tianjin, inquiring about the situation of a certain French industrial and commercial export. The consulate's replies are often inevitably lacking in detail. It has been found that the Stendhal Printing House in Paris publishes a graphic index of French exports every year, which includes texts in French, English, Spanish, Portuguese, Italian, and Dutch, and is divided into categories such as food, woodware, jewelry, spices, clothing, machinery, entertainment products, and paper products. It is very detailed. Therefore, a copy has been purchased and sent to the Ministry of Industry for forwarding to the Ministry of Industry so that our merchants engaged in French import and export can directly send letters to the Ministry of Industry for inquiry. This will not only enable them to obtain all the information but also save time. Accordingly, the original graphic index is enclosed for your Ministry to check and reserve for use. The enclosed graphic index of French exports is approved. In addition to forwarding the original document to the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Visitation Bureau for storage and reference, if the Association wishes to inquire about the situation of French industrial and commercial exports in the future, you may send a letter directly to the Bureau for inquiry. This order is hereby issued.

Telegram Received by the Red Cross for Relief in Changge

The Chinese Red Cross received a telegram from the Henan Relief Association, which stated: To the Chinese Red Cross: It has been repeatedly reported by Tang Ji, the magistrate of Changge County, and Gao Yihao, the representative of the 25th District, that after the banditry in the county, Fan Zhongyou, Liu Guitang, Sun Shigui, Hui Yingqi, and others, totaling more than 200,000 people, stationed themselves in the territory for seven months, carrying out indiscriminate looting and exhausting all resources. According to statistics, the forced contributions of funds, firewood, and grass, converted to silver, amounted to no less than one million yuan. More than 6,000 laborers were conscripted, more than 5,000 livestock were seized, and more than 1,900 carts were taken. Countless properties were lost. In addition, there was a severe drought throughout the year, and the wheat crop withered. In addition to the deaths and displacement, there are more than 5,000 extremely poor families who cannot afford to cook. Each household is deeply suffering from banditry, drought, and war. They cannot plan for the next day. We earnestly implore you to show compassion for the survivors and bestow your benevolence to help them survive. We are deeply grateful. Zhang Fangdong of the Henan Relief Association.

New Locomotive Passenger Cars on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Are Being Installed and Put into Service

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau previously found that the original locomotives were too old and lacked traction, which inevitably caused delays in train schedules. Therefore, in order to fundamentally address the problem, it purchased eight Pacific-type new locomotives from the United Kingdom. These new locomotives have been successively installed and tested, and the results have been very satisfactory. Four of them have now been allocated for use on special express trains. The remaining locomotives will be used on express trains. In the future, train delays will not occur again unless there are unforeseen circumstances.

After the new locomotives are put into service, the travel time between Beijing and Shanghai can be shortened. However, the entire line is single-track, and the old sleepers along the way are a major obstacle to increasing speed. The Railway Bureau has now begun to urgently replace the rotten sleepers. It is planned to revise the timetable from March 1. Currently, the special express train between Beijing and Shanghai takes 7 hours and 20 minutes. This will be reduced to 6 hours and 45 minutes in the future. The night special express train will depart from Beijing and Shanghai at 11:30 p.m. and arrive at the station at 7:20 a.m. When the old sleepers have been completely replaced, further shortening will be attempted. The problem of the shortage of passenger cars can also be gradually resolved. It is heard that the Wusong Factory of the Railway is now installing and putting into service two first- and second-class combined cars and five third-class cars from among the newly arrived passenger cars. After they have been completely manufactured, these new passenger cars will be formed into two special express trains running between Beijing and Shanghai in order to facilitate travel.

Good News for Creditors of the Rising Sun Bank

▲Hot Spring Bathhouse and Others in Contact for Sale

▲Partial Debt Repayment as Soon as Possible

The Rising Sun Bank and the Da Shi Jie (Great World) Savings Department are still being liquidated by accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang. This reporter interviewed accountant Wu yesterday, who said that in terms of the various assets, if they can be properly disposed of, creditors can hopefully avoid losses, but it is only a matter of time before they can be repaid. The first step is to sell the branch locations of the Rising Sun Bank on Zhejiang Road and Sichuan Road. The Hot Spring Bathhouse and other properties are also in the process of being sold. Today (i.e., yesterday), letters have been sent to urge the repayment of debts, and the funds received will be deposited in reliable banks to repay the principal of savings deposits and current deposits as soon as possible within the year. The next step is to repay the principal of fixed deposits and current account deposits, and finally to clear the interest. Regarding the private assets of Huang Chujiu, an agreement has been reached with lawyer Tan Yigong to publicly discuss the disposal method or repay in installments after the registration is completed within two weeks. Currently, the Rising Sun Bank head office has retained eight original staff members to be responsible for handling affairs, and the branches have retained about three people each, as is the case with the Great World Savings Department, in order to save money. This reporter also interviewed lawyer Tan Yigong yesterday, who expressed great dissatisfaction with the disunity and chaotic opinions of the creditor group. He also said that Huang's private assets are sufficient to cover the debts. After the cleaning and registration are completed within two weeks, the details will be fully disclosed to the press, so creditors can rest assured.

The Sensational "Daredevil" Case Ends

▲Hong Shen Withdraws Lawsuit Yesterday

Last spring, the Grand Cathay Cinema screened the film "Daredevil" starring American Rock, the content of which was extremely insulting to the Chinese people. Hong Shen, a professor at Fudan University, went to see it and was filled with righteous indignation. He gave a speech on stage in front of the audience, causing the audience to return their tickets in droves. Gao Yongqing, the manager of the cinema, accused Hong of disrupting order and had him arrested and detained in the Xinzha Police Station, but he was soon released. In addition to reporting the matter to the central government through the municipal party headquarters to lodge a protest with the United States to ban the film, Hong also hired lawyers Zhan Jifeng and Wu Chengyu to sue Gao Yongqing in the former Provisional Court. After a trial, the Provisional Court was reorganized and the case was transferred to the Special District Local Court. Later, summonses were issued, but because there was hope for a settlement, it was temporarily suspended for nearly ten months. The news subsided, and the public's enthusiasm for the matter waned as time passed. Moreover, it was rumored that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs had reached a satisfactory result in its negotiations with the United States, so the matter was largely forgotten. However, the Special Court suddenly issued a summons yesterday afternoon, and few people outside knew about it, so at 2:00 PM, the audience seats were empty, far from the grandeur of the previous trial. Even the defendant was not present. Only the plaintiff, Hong Shen, and his lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, arrived at the court on time. Judge Zhou Baiming took his seat, and lawyer Zhan stood up and applied to withdraw the lawsuit, saying that the case had now been resolved peacefully outside the court. Hong Shen's purpose in filing the lawsuit was to ban the screening of the film and to have the defendant publish an apology to the plaintiff in the newspaper and donate a large sum of 5,000 gold dollars to the school. Now that all of these goals have been achieved, there is no personal interest involved, and the party headquarters has already taken appropriate action. He requested that the court grant the withdrawal of the lawsuit in order to bring an end to the matter. Judge Zhou approved the request and dismissed the case, thus ending this sensational and protracted case.

The Gatekeeper of Lin Weiqing's House Was Indeed in Collusion with Kidnappers

▲Secret Meeting at the Tiannan Hotel Beforehand

▲Reporting the Owner's Time of Arrival and Departure

Lin Weiqing, a Cantonese contractor residing at 55 Baker Road, returned to his residence at 1:10 AM the day before yesterday with his wife and daughter in his own car. As they arrived at the gate, the gatekeeper was slow to open the gate, which allowed kidnappers who were lying in wait to seize the opportunity. Lin, being alert, drove the car into the house, but his wife and daughter were taken away. The car suddenly stopped midway, and the kidnappers were unable to escape together. Lin's wife and daughter were fortunate to return home. They reported to the police station that the gatekeeper was suspected. The details of the investigation have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that Lin Weiqing is the brother of Lin Biao, the current president of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The gatekeeper he hired, named Wang JiaKui, is from Shandong. According to the police investigation, he was indeed involved in collusion with the bandits. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Special District Local Court, where he was interrogated by Judge Xiao. According to the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin, the defendant Wang JiaKui has confessed to the police that on the 1st and 2nd of this month, he and his accomplices secretly met at the Tiannan Hotel on Avenue Edward VII to inform his accomplices of the time his master entered and left the house. The day before yesterday, the bandits were lying in ambush near Lin's house. Lin's driver honked the horn of the car frequently from a distance of several tens of paces from the residence, but the defendant pretended not to hear. It is believed that the defendant harbored this malicious intent because his request to his employer for a wage increase was denied. Lin Weiqing then arrived in court to testify that he had hired Wang as a gatekeeper for over a year, with a monthly salary of 18 yuan, which, together with additional income, amounted to about 24 gold dollars per month. He did not notice any bad behavior on his part in the past. The night before yesterday, he returned home with his wife and daughter from his relatives' house. As the car arrived in front of the gate, he honked the horn repeatedly, but the defendant delayed opening the gate, causing four bandits to rush out from the west. One of them held a pistol and used the butt of the gun to smash the car window glass. He realized that they were not good people and got out of the car and ran into the house first, pushing one of the bandits down. His wife and daughter were then kidnapped, but they soon returned together. After careful consideration, he suspected the defendant. He questioned the defendant, who claimed that he was slow to open the door because of a foot ailment and that he needed to find the key. Someone invited him to the Tiannan Hotel to inquire about the owner's whereabouts, intending to carry out a kidnapping, and asked him to join their party, but he did not agree, and so on. The court ordered the defendant to be detained and the hearing postponed.

▲A Clever Plan to Compete in the Shipping Industry

In order to compete in the shipping industry, the Japanese Mail Steamship Company is imitating the American steamship companies and is switching to female stewards on board. A Sand Boat Outside Wusongkou is Robbed by Bandits

▲Another Sand Boat Luckily Escaped Due to Favorable Winds

Yesterday morning, a northern sand boat entered the port. According to the boat crew, at about 4 PM the day before yesterday, the boat was sailing through the Tongsha waters outside Wusongkou. At the same time, two other sand boats were sailing behind them. Suddenly, five bandit boats appeared on the sea, rushed towards the boat, and fired shots to intimidate them, hoping to rob them. Fortunately, the northeast wind was very strong at the time, and the boat crew noticed this, quickly raised the sails, and sailed quickly with the wind, thus avoiding being caught up by the bandit boats and escaping danger. However, seeing the previous boat escape, the bandits quickly surrounded the two sand boats behind them. The two boats seemed not to have noticed beforehand, so they could not escape. After the boat sailed away from the bandit boats, they saw the two sand boats behind them surrounded by bandit boats from a distance, and they heard intermittent gunfire. It is likely that the two sand boats had self-defense weapons on board and resisted the bandit boats in the face of danger. Later, the boat sailed further away and no longer heard gunfire. The boat entered the port yesterday morning, but the two sand boats were not seen by noon. It is thought that they have all been robbed by the bandit boats.

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Announces the Reason for Salty Tap Water

▲No Harm to Drinking

The tap water in Zhabei often has a salty taste at this time of year, and citizens often do not understand the reason and misunderstand. Recently, someone asked the Municipal Health Bureau about the cause of the salty tap water and whether it is harmful to drinking. According to the bureau, the reason for the salty taste is actually due to the low water level of the river, which allows seawater to intrude. A strong salty taste also occurred two years ago. The saltiest day was January 9, 1929, when the salt content reached more than 2,700 parts per million, which took three weeks to subside. In the past few days of this year, a salty taste has been detected again. The highest salt content in the water is also more than 2,000 parts per million. On the 5th of this month, the Municipal Health Laboratory sampled the water for testing, and the salt content was still 985 parts per million, which is far different from the usual 20 parts per million, resulting in a very salty taste. However, the number of bacteria and the amount of *E. coli* in the water, as well as other chemical components, are still the same as usual and still meet the Shanghai drinking water hygiene standards, so there is no harm to drinking. As for the salty taste in the tap water, there is currently no scientific method to remove it. However, the intrusion of seawater into the river is very short each year, so it is expected to recover soon.

Pirates Rob Fabric

▲Shipowner Wounded

▲Loss of Five Thousand Taels

Fang Ji, a fabric merchant from Chonghai, hired Wang Maolang's Chongsha boat to transport 500 packages of fabric to Shanghai for sale. Wu, a clerk from the shop, was assigned to escort the goods. On the 5th, while sailing on the Jiwo Port waters of Tongzhou, two pirate boats suddenly appeared and fired shots to order them to stop. Two of Wang's crew members were wounded by bullets. Wang had no choice but to lower the sail and stop the boat. The pirates swarmed onto the boat and robbed all the silver dollars. Not satisfied, they forced Wang's boat to sail to Tongzhou, with the two pirate boats following and monitoring them. When they sailed to a seaport, they were forced to dock, and the fabric on the boat was moved to the two pirate boats. When Wu saw the pirates moving the fabric, he pleaded with them to stop, but this angered the pirates, who shot him in the back. The two pirate boats then sailed away into the East China Sea. Wang's boat has now sailed to the mouth of the Liu River and sent Wu and the two crew members to the hospital for treatment. One of the crew members is in critical condition. Yesterday, Wang came to Shanghai to report the incident. The fabric merchants immediately telegraphed the Chonghai shop to inform them and began taking stock of the fabric. It is reported that the stolen fabric is worth 5,000 taels.

Wife Denies Husband

▲Luo Wenyi and Sun Huaiying Compete for Wife

Luo Wenyi, a villager from Haizhou, is 32 years old and has been farming in the countryside for a living. His wife, Wang, is currently 31 years old. Luo was engaged to her when he was seven years old, and she was brought into his family as a child bride. They grew up together and were quite harmonious. At the age of 21, they officially married, and the love between the couple was very strong. She worked diligently alongside her husband, farming the land. However, in the first month of the lunar calendar last year, Wang was suddenly abducted by a fellow villager and disappeared without a trace. Luo searched everywhere without success. After repeated investigations, he learned from Wang Jiayou, a relative of Wang working in Shanghai, that Wang had become acquainted with a fellow villager named Sun and was cohabitating with him behind Xinsen Lane, Caojiadu, West Shanghai. Wang Jiayou immediately sent a letter to Luo. Luo, along with his brother-in-law Wang Hongzhi, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday. Yesterday afternoon at about 2:00 PM, Luo and Wang Jiayou and others went to the 6th District Police Station to report the incident. The police immediately dispatched officers along with the complainants to the address. At the time, Wang and her paramour Sun Huaiying were both taken back to the station. District Chief Ren interrogated the accused. The plaintiff Luo Wenyi testified that he was 32 years old, and the rest of his testimony was as described above. Wang Jiayou testified that he was 27 years old and from Taizhou, and that Wang was indeed Luo's wife, and that Sun Huaiying had abducted her and they were cohabitating was true. Wang Hongzhi testified that he was 27 years old, from Taizhou, and that Wang was his sister and had married Luo Wenyi. The defendant Wang falsely claimed that her surname was Sun and her given name was Xi, that she was 31 years old, that she and Sun Huaiying were husband and wife, and that she did not know Luo Wenyi. Sun Huaiying testified that he was 28 years old, that Wang was his wife, and the rest of his testimony was vague. After hearing the testimonies, District Chief Ren believed that Wang had her younger brother and husband present as witnesses, yet she dared to deny the facts, which was truly despicable. She was sentenced to be sent to court for trial after the documents were prepared.

On his way back, he encountered a Japanese policeman from the Jing'an Temple Police Station and told him what had happened. The Japanese policeman rushed to investigate and reported it to the Japanese Consulate. The next morning, the four men were arrested. It is heard that one was surnamed Goto, one was surnamed Kazuno, one was surnamed Aino, and one was surnamed Matsumoto. They had arrived in Shanghai with Yamamoto on the Shanghai Maru on the 30th of last month. Because they knew each other, after landing, the four men stayed at the Katsuta Hotel, and Yamamoto stayed at the Hinomaru Hotel. Soon after, they rented a house together in the French Concession. It is not known why, but a tragic murder occurred. Yamamoto has now been transferred to the Fukumin Hospital and is not in danger of death. The four assailants are being detained at the Japanese Consulate, where the case is being investigated.

Rental Dispute in the French Concession's Dexing, Zhizhong, and Lixian Neighborhoods

▲Social Bureau Orders Original Plan to be Followed

The Shanghai French Concession Tenants' Association presented a petition to the Municipal Government regarding the private collection of small rents and the raising of rent by the Tongren Fuyuantang for the houses in Dexing, Zhizhong, and Lixian Neighborhoods, requesting that the Municipal Government order them to voluntarily reduce the rent. The Municipal Government instructed the Social Bureau to investigate and handle the matter. The bureau stated that the collection of small rents had long been prohibited, and that the Tongren Fuyuantang, as a well-known charity organization, should not charge extra fees. The bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate. According to the organization, it had collected donations for charitable activities from tenants in Zhizhong and Lixian Neighborhoods and had reduced rents in the past. An investigation revealed that the houses were built with borrowed funds, and the rental income was used to repay the debts. The organization had already specified the distribution of rental income from the three neighborhoods when applying for construction, which was related to the loan guarantee and should not be changed arbitrarily to affect the debt. As for the donation issue, the bureau had no records to verify. However, since the tenants voluntarily paid donations in the past, why did they now complain about it? Was it a deliberate attempt to resist rent or was there some other reason? It was impossible to speculate. Furthermore, the increase or decrease in the income of charitable organizations is related to the rise and fall of relief efforts. It is not permissible to arbitrarily abandon the legitimate interests of public property. Moreover, houses should be rented out after a contract is signed. Some tenants in Zhizhong and other neighborhoods moved in before signing a contract, and some regretted after signing a contract, which was not appropriate. It is heard that in addition to submitting a report, the bureau has ordered the Shanghai Charitable Organization to collect rent from the Zhizhong and Lixian neighborhoods starting from January 1 of this year according to the contract and not allow tenants to delay payment for any reason, so as to prevent abuses. Those who have not signed a contract should be required to sign a supplementary contract within a limited time. The five-year validity period was also not included in the original plan. The organization was also ordered to report the handling situation truthfully for verification.

New World Property Rent Lawsuit

▲Is it Five Thousand Taels or Five Thousand Dollars?

▲The Court Orders Advance Payment of 10,000 Yuan

The New World Amusement Park at the Mud City Bridge Pier stopped operating after the May Thirtieth Massacre. It was rented to British military authorities to garrison British troops for several years. Until the winter before last year, when the British troops stationed in Shanghai withdrew, it was still used as an entertainment venue. A foreigner leased it from the landlord, Yuan Ji Agency, for a monthly rent of five thousand taels. Three months later, Xu Yaoxiang took over the entertainment business and defaulted on the rent since May of last year. By September, for five months, not a penny was paid. Yuan Ji sued Xu in the Special District Court, seeking to recover 25,000 taels in back rent. Xu argued that the monthly rent was not five thousand taels, but five thousand yuan. After the debate concluded, Xu lost the case. Dissatisfied, Xu filed an appeal. The second instance has not yet been decided, and the rent has been in arrears for another four months from October to January of this year. Yuan Ji sued again. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhou Daren of the Special Court summoned the defendant, who hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to defend, saying that when the plaintiff rented the house to a foreigner, the monthly rent was indeed five thousand taels of silver. Later, when the defendant continued the lease, he made it clear to the landlord that it was a long-term lease, not a short-term rent like that of a foreigner. He requested that the silver amount be changed to the dollar amount. Although no lease was signed, many people knew about it. Therefore, the previous months were paid at five thousand yuan each time, but the landlord still issued rent receipts for five thousand taels. He requested corrections, but the landlord said that the amount on the rent receipt was greater than the amount paid by the tenant, which did not harm the tenant. Therefore, he did not insist on changing it. Unexpectedly, after a few months, the landlord used the rent receipts as evidence to demand a monthly rent of five thousand taels from the tenant. The means are truly cunning, and so on. Chen Jingbo, the accountant of Yuan Ji Agency, testified that the monthly rent was indeed five thousand taels, paid in advance. The defendant initially paid five thousand taels for several months, and so on. He also hired a lawyer to argue. Judge Zhou advised both parties to reconcile. Before a final judgment is made on the appeal in the previous case, the defendant was ordered to temporarily pay five thousand yuan per month. After the appeal case is finalized, if five thousand taels must be paid, then it will be made up month by month. As for the four months of rent owed in this case, totaling 20,000 yuan, the defendant was ordered to pay 10,000 yuan within the old year and 10,000 yuan by the end of January next year. Starting from February in the solar calendar, monthly payments must be made as scheduled, without delay. Both parties followed the court order and settled the case.

Automobile News Column

The Useless Depression of the American Automobile Industry by Cheng Zhizheng

▲The Depression is Due to the Business Cycle

▲A Three-Year Cycle May Turn This Year

▲Forsdike Announces Relief Plan

▲President Hoover Also Cannot Prevent It

Not long ago. I (the original author refers to himself, and the following will follow this usage) went to attend the annual meeting of automotive engineers in this city. Originally. Every time the annual meeting came around. Everyone was always very happy. Even if there was any speech. It was nothing more than telling humorous and funny stories. Or reporting happy memories of the past year. But this year's annual meeting. But it was very different. Everyone met and talked about the depression. And during the meeting. Everyone was silent. With a double-locked frown. The air around suddenly changed from pleasant to bleak. This thing is really amazing.

Especially interesting. Was a few of the speeches. They all thought that business had reached a terrible point. And this depression. I don't know when it will end. One of them said it most comically. He said. "If you have something to do. Then. I advise you not to easily leave it. Because once you leave it. You will immediately have nothing to do. In other words. It is also to join the ranks of the unemployed. If you are really unfortunate and leave your job. You should not wait for opportunities in the city. Go back to the countryside to see the cattle and sheep. Wait until the period of commercial revival. Then come out again." At that time. Everyone listened and couldn't help but feel sad.

In order to participate in this annual meeting. I couldn't help but think of things from the past. When in December 1914. The European War broke out. Everyone was worried. Thinking that the entire European market would fall. And that the losses would be incalculable. However. After a few months. Not only was the United States' trade with Europe unaffected. And it suddenly took off. Breaking the unprecedented record. The reason is that during the war, the production tools of various countries. Were transformed into munitions. Unable to supply the needs. The United States took the opportunity to gain a lot of benefits. In 1921. The commercial depression was brewed again. But after three or four months. It returned to its original state. If we calculate from 1880. To 1930. Then. In these fifty-two years. The years of depression are as follows. 1884丨5 years. 1893丨4 years. 1896丨7丨8 years. 1904. 1908. 192 years. 1914. 1921. 1924. 1927.

There are also times when the depression. Is due to psychological effects. For example, after the end of the Great War in 1919. Everyone thought that the treaties between the Allied countries. Would be abolished uniformly. The war debts are also not recognized. In this way. Commerce will inevitably suffer damage. So as soon as the rumors started. The customers didn't dare to buy too much either. The factory didn't dare to produce too much either. How could anyone know that the Allied countries' war debts. Were not cancelled. Instead, they rushed to place orders everywhere. This belongs to the psychologically caused depression.

This phenomenon of prosperity and decline. Is called the business cycle in commerce. Its nature is like winter and summer. It is cyclical. It can also be compared to the tide. It is constantly circulating. A year or two ago. Some optimistic car merchants. Sang a high pitch. Said that the theory of the business cycle. Has been broken. In the future, the United States will definitely be able to maintain satisfactory results every year. And continue to develop forward. But what about now. The depression is finally here again. Who can explain that it is not due to the law of the business cycle.

The business cycle is especially prominent in automobiles. If we look at it with a graph. Then. Sometimes it increases and sometimes it decreases. It is like an iron law. Although we say that the business cycle can be compared to the tides and seasons. However, there is one fundamental difference. Because the tides and seasons can have a certain period of time. Can be predictable. And the business cycle. Is impossible to predict. It has neither a fixed interval of years. There is no same situation before and after. Generally speaking, before a major business depression. There are a few things that are most obvious. The stock must fall in price. Prices are lowered. At the same time, interest rates also fall sharply from high to low. Similarly, at the beginning of the recovery period. The stock rises first. Then many things also follow it high.

Last year, the securities in the United States fell terribly. This year, more than a thousand banks have collapsed again. This depression has begun. Last fall. When the market was sluggish. The President of the United States, Hoover, convened a meeting with the automotive tycoon Ford and other leaders in the business world to discuss countermeasures. And several methods were agreed upon. However, it was ultimately ineffective. Industry and commerce. Gradually sinking. But when can it be recovered. No one can make a definitive statement. Some people say. Judging from history. The current depression. May be about to recover. Because from the beginning to now. It has been sixteen months. There is no reason not to turn around. But from the perspective of experts, this special cycle. Cannot recover until the end of 1931. After generally discussing the depression in the United States. I will talk about the automobile itself. If according to experts' estimates. Then. In 1931, the automobile industry. Will of course also be trapped in the depression. However. The prosperity and decline of the automobile industry. Although it cannot completely get rid of the business cycle. However, it also has some special points. The increase and decrease in the automobile industry. Is about once every three years. After the end of the three years. The following year. Must be the year of the most development in the industry. From a historical point of view. 1921 was a year of reduced production. In 1922, it created an unprecedented record. Now 1927 to 1930 were all years of reduced production. Calculated, it has been exactly three years. 1931 may have

Flying Display Factory's Large Press Machine - Auspicious

Often the panels, edges, or rear ends of automobile bodies show uneven places, which are very unsightly. This is not a defect in the paint material, but because the steel was not in compliance with the law when it was formed. If pure steel plates are used and pressed with a fine machine, there will be no such defects. The Flying Display Body Factory of the General Motors Manufacturing Plant in the United States has recently installed a large new press hinge machine, which is specially used for pressing and refreshing steel sheets. The old style could only press one piece at a time, but now even two or three pieces can be done at the same time. And its results are far better than before.

The press machine shown in the picture is more accurate and exquisite than other types. The Flying Display Factory now has 14 of these machines, each weighing 400 tons. And it has a pressure of 1,300 tons. It can simultaneously generate four kinds of significant sliding movements at a time. Therefore, it is called a four-sided sliding press hinge machine.

This new four-sided sliding press machine can make large steel sheets with the shortest joints. Therefore, the surface is not only smooth and flat, but also has no uneven ripples. And its overall strength is stronger than other long-section press machines.

The steel plate produced by the large press machine has a clean surface and accurate curvature. Therefore, the base of the car body made by the Flying Display Factory is of excellent quality and has a beautiful appearance. This is why General Motors is satisfied.

This machine has strong capabilities and is competent to press the hardest and most bulky steel. However, its working time is shortened and the cost is saved. Compared with the old-style machines, it is about ten times more. Therefore, General Motors customers also get economic benefits.

Special development.

However. One thing is worth noting. Is that the current automobile market. Is a "replacement market" rather than a "new purchase market." What does this mean. At present, the automobile industry in the United States and even Europe. 橤职 is developed. Almost one in every four or five people has a car. So unless the old car is broken. Don't buy a new car. It is called "replacement market." Rather than a "new purchase market." The development of the replacement market. Is ultimately very limited. Unless you really create a "new purchase market." The automobile industry. It is ultimately difficult to create an unprecedented record. So I dare say. The automobile trade in 1931. May be better than 1930. However. It is not the most victorious year. In short. The current world depression. Is a natural cycle. It is not a novel strange thing. As for the automobile industry. It is indeed governed by natural cycles. But its law of cycle is different from ordinary business. It is probably once every three years. Counting to 1931, it should recover. But because automobiles in the United States have reached their highest point. The development in 1931. Is still in the "replacement market." I also talked about this matter with Rubber King Forsdike. I asked him what he thought. Mr. Forsdike smiled and said. "I have a way. That is, everyone should build more cheap and beautiful cars." He also said, "The manufacturers have been really anxious these months. Now there is no other way. Only find ways to improve the goods.

News

Miscellaneous Road Administration News from Various Provinces - Wu Fei

▲ Jiangsu Province: Jiangsu Province is actively and tirelessly engaged in conscripting labor for road construction. The most important recent projects are approximately as follows: (1) The Department of Construction is prioritizing the construction of the Provincial-Ju Road, specifically a section of about ten li from the provincial capital's train station to Huiyuan Temple. For the Jing-Wu Road, it is prioritizing a section of about ten li from Andong Gate in Jiangning to Tiexin Bridge. Simultaneously, it is strictly ordering all counties to continue conscripting labor for road construction, setting deadlines for completing roads jointly managed by the province and counties. (2) The Zhen-Hu Provincial Road within Jiading County is planned to be forty-five li long. The Department of Construction has set a deadline for completion by the end of the 19th year of the Republic. (3) The Fengxian County Construction Bureau considers the Min-Nan Road an important transportation artery for the county. The National Roads Association is planning to construct a motor road from Minhang to Pinghu, which also has a practical need for connection. Approval has been obtained from the Department of Construction to commence operations imminently. The funding will be reallocated from the collected road and land taxes. Bidding has already begun, with a three-month deadline for completion. (4) The area from Xinfeng to Huangxu in Zhenjiang is extremely important for transportation. The Construction Bureau plans to construct a new road immediately. Surveying work has already been completed, and construction is expected to begin soon.

▲ Zhejiang Province: The most recent road administration plans in Zhejiang Province involve two matters: (1) Regarding the originally planned Yan-Hui Highway, the Highway Bureau dispatched engineers to form a survey team, which has already completed the survey. The Bureau has decided to construct a road of over three hundred li, starting from Yanzhou and passing through Fuyang, Xindeng, Fenshui, and Liang'an counties. Construction is scheduled to begin this month, with the road expected to be open to traffic by next summer. (2) The Hangzhou Electric Bureau's plan to lay tram tracks was approved by the Construction Conference. The Bureau will remain responsible for handling the procedures. It is reported that the estimated cost for laying crushed stone, purchasing steel rails, and trams is approximately two million two hundred thousand yuan, and efforts are underway to raise the funds.

▲ Anhui Province: Since the opening of the Wu-Dang section of the Jing-Wu Motor Road, managed by the Anhui Department of Construction, travel for merchants has been quite smooth. However, due to river obstructions at Daqiao Town, the junction of Wu and Dang, vehicles must stop at the station and transfer to another vehicle to cross the river, which is extremely inconvenient. A plan for a temporary bridge has been drafted and submitted to the Department of Construction for approval. Construction began on the first day of last month, and it has been completed day and night. From now on, long-distance buses departing from Wuhu will be able to reach Dangtu directly within an hour.

▲ Guangdong Province: The Guang-Shan Highway in Guangdong Province is being constructed in sections, and the entire road is nearing completion. Several dozen vehicles are currently operating on the first trunk line, the Zhang-Hui section, the Ping-Hui section, the Hai-Lu section, the Lu-Pu section, the Pu-Jie section, the Jie-An section, and the Bo-Xiang section, which are all open to traffic. The Pu'ning to Shantou section and the Chao'an to Huanggang section of the eastern trunk line are also open to traffic. Among the eastern second trunk lines, the forty-li section from Boluo to Heyuan that has not been constructed, and the twenty li along the river and forty li on the south bank of the river from Heyuan to Longchuan, are all open to traffic. However, the sections from Longchuan to Laolong, Qiling to Languan, and Dabu to Fengshi have been surveyed and are currently under construction in sequence.

▲ Hubei Province: The Hubei Department of Construction is also very active in developing various highways. (1) The Han-Yi Line was constructed to Shayang by the end of last year. (2) The E-Dong Line was constructed to Macheng. (3) Bridges on the E-Bei Line are being repaired, and eighteen long-distance gas-powered vehicles are being added, requiring an estimated expense of one hundred and sixty thousand yuan. (4) Currently, only the Hanyangmen section of the Yangtze River Road can be constructed. Completion of the entire road will require an estimated expense of over two hundred thousand yuan. Construction will be completed in phases once the Department of Finance allocates the construction funds.

▲ Sichuan Province: Sichuan Province plans to construct the Qian-Yu Road from Chongqing to Guizhou Province and has obtained the agreement of the Guizhou Provincial Government. The entire road is over four hundred li long, with an estimated cost of five thousand yuan per li, totaling two million yuan. Construction will be carried out by conscripting labor. Engineers have been dispatched to survey the route, with a deadline of three months for completion. Construction is expected to begin in the fourth month and is projected to be completed in two years, providing direct access to Guizhou and Guangxi provinces.

▲ Xinjiang Province: Xinjiang Province is located in the remote northwest, with vast deserts and rugged roads. It is appropriate to start with transportation. Therefore, the original official roads are being slightly repaired to serve as motor roads. However, due to poor road conditions, vehicles are frequently damaged. The provincial government has appointed a commissioner and hired engineers to conduct a preliminary survey. The motor road from Dihua to Gucheng is four hundred and seventy-three li long, with an estimated cost of over one thousand taels of provincial silver. Meanwhile, personnel have been dispatched to supervise the construction, and three thousand engineering soldiers are being allocated from various regiments stationed in the Dihua-Gucheng area, divided into four groups, to begin construction. The construction of the roads from Gucheng to Hami and Xingxing Gorge will follow sequentially.

▲ Jilin Province: Jilin Province has the Ji-Hai, Ji-Chang, and Ji-Dun roads open to traffic. There are very few cars. Recently, the Construction Bureau plans to build highways, sending personnel to various counties to investigate, survey, and construct, so that minerals can be exploited, industries developed, and transportation facilitated in all seasons.

The above covers the provinces that are known. Other provinces will be discussed in further installments as information becomes available.

Youth Corner

Suppressing Bandits - Ke Ci

That morning, at only four o'clock, A-Da was awakened by a rustling sound. He thought, "Here they come again." Indeed, recently rats had often been making noise in their room at night, not only disturbing their sleep but also gnawing a large piece out of the spine of A-Da's newly bought book. This was what A-Da hated the most.

There was really no way to deal with it. A-Da had bought a mousetrap, hoping to reduce the number of rats, but coincidentally, these rats wouldn't eat the bait, so it had no chance to work. A-Da had to seal the rat holes, hoping to prevent the rats from coming out, but the rats' abilities were truly vast. Before long, they immediately reopened a hole. A-Da thought, perhaps if he got a cat, the rats wouldn't come out again, right? A cat was found soon after, but it didn't work either. Often, even the cat's food at night was eaten by the rats. A-Da had no choice but to stare blankly at the rat hole, gnashing his teeth and thinking.

"Here they come again," A-Da said to himself after being awakened by the sound of rats gnawing on things. "I'm going to give you a taste of your own medicine." So he got up silently, sealed the rat holes, closed the door, and then—

"A-Er, get up, help me catch rats," he said, turning on the light.

Their only weapons were iron hooks and iron pokers. The rats were driven out of the bookshelf by them and ran frantically around the room, making it impossible for A-Da and A-Er to hit them. Finally, "Let's pile the boxes into a corner and trap the rats inside, then it will be easy to hit the dummies," A-Da came up with an idea and suggested doing that. After passing the suggestion, they piled the boxes up, forming a corner with the wall.

"You wait here, if the rat comes, you hit it," A-Da instructed A-Er. He himself went around the room chasing them. The rats were actually chased into the corner. A-Er struck, but missed. The rat ran onto the wall. A-Da aimed and rushed over with a strike. With a crash, it was sure to hit. Just one hit would knock the rat down. But no, he only made a hole in the wall. Another strike, and he still missed. By this time, he was laughing so hard he couldn't close his mouth. He thought, he was actually fighting the rats like he was suppressing bandits. The rats, at this time, disappeared, hiding somewhere.

Searching, searching everywhere. Under the bed, under the table, in the bookshelf, in the corner—they searched everywhere, but they couldn't find the "fugitive" rat.

"Maybe it slipped away through that hole,"

"No, all the holes in this room are sealed,"

"Then where did it go?"

"Search again, it can't have left the room,"

A-Da took a flashlight and searched everywhere, but still nothing. Finally—

"Ah, here it is!" When he shone the light behind the bookshelf, he discovered a rat hiding in a pile of magazines. He unceremoniously struck it with a stick—he had now switched to a stick—and hit it. He really hit it, but because of the books blocking the way, the rat wasn't hurt and instead charged out, startling A-Da.

"Oh, there are two of them, there are two of them!"

"It's really strange, when there were none, there weren't even one, but now that there are some, there are two." They chased, the rats fled, but they still couldn't hurt them.

"Come quickly, come quickly, I've got a rat trapped!" A-Er shouted. At this time, one of the rats was trapped by him with the window, but the rat was still able to move. It climbed out of the gap, onto the edge of the wall. A-Da struck it with a stick, knocking it onto the bookshelf, and then another strike ended its life. A-Da triumphantly pulled it out from behind the bookshelf. "Can you still run now, Mr. Rat?" A-Da said involuntarily, feeling the tension of his spirit, the contraction of his muscles, and the joy of revenge. But immediately, he thought, if he were being chased and beaten to near death, how resentful and sad would he be? He couldn't help but pity it.

But this thought disappeared immediately, and they began to catch the second one. The second one was actually captured alive, having been pinned down by a hot water bottle. Without hesitation, A-Da picked it up and stuffed it into the spittoon. That rat was "executed" in this way. They carried it outside, dug a hole, and buried it.

The next day, A-Er said, "My hand got cut last night." A-Da didn't say anything. He was lying in bed, panting—he had caught a cold last night.

After Unemployment - Hui

The pain that unemployment brings to a person is like a heavy fog descending upon a ship at sea. Even with a powerful engine and a clever, experienced captain, there is nothing that can be done. I am young, strong, and fairly intelligent, and I have enjoyed a considerable amount of education through my own efforts. But life is sneering and mocking me, a drifter with no power in society. I haven't had a day of peace. The life of this society has given me a lot of training. I will try my best to scrape and bow to find any job to do. I don't dislike any job because it's too unpalatable or too humiliating to my talent, just like my poor stomach. I swallow whatever food I get, without ever disliking the sweet, sour, bitter, or spicy. However, the jobs that I can find with my meager strength are always short-term jobs like repairing roads. The road collapses, they ask you to repair it. Once it's repaired, I'm back to being a wandering vagrant on the road.

The weather these days is severely cold, with white clouds pressing down on the sky. The sharp wind is howling everywhere. You don't need to be a prophet to know that it will snow soon. The cold doesn't limit my work ethic. Even heavy clouds and rain are like mild, sunny skies to me. But when I return to my small room, wandering the streets like a homeless dog because I can't find a job, I suddenly feel exhausted, like a bow that has lost its string. I lie on the bed, staring at the ceiling, without even wanting to look at the books I enjoy reading. Besides, the easy-to-digest books have all been read in the past few days. All that's left are a few stiff theoretical books. I fully feel that everything is unfriendly to me, everything is sneering at me.

Normally, I always sleep at midnight and get up at seven in the morning to work. But now I'm completely out of sync. I even go to sleep six hours early. When dusk peeks into my window, I can sleep until eleven o'clock the next day, like ordinary Shanghai people. It's as if getting up at this time is still too early. I lazily go to get some hot water to wash my face.

Sometimes I think, "Oh, this is too decadent." "No, no," I reply forcefully, "it's because I feel like there's nothing to do."

Lu Xianzhen (Bing), a strong basketball player from Southeast China.
